Page 23

1934.08.11

Three-Nation Military Exercises

Frequent Gunfire Creates Tense Atmosphere

American Troops to Proceed to Yuguan Soon

Sentries Deployed at All Barracks in Qinhuangdao

British Troops to Hold Second Exercise, with More Units Participating

(Tianjin) The Japanese garrison in Qinhuangdao has been conducting combat exercises outside their camp by the sea for several days. The participating troops include communications, medical, artillery, and infantry units. The exercises have been held for two days, from the 8th to the 9th. On the 9th, 240 American soldiers arrived in Qinhuangdao from Tianjin and coordinated with local American troops to conduct field exercises at 7:00 AM on the 10th. Additionally, a unit of French Annamese soldiers was also conducting target practice by the sea. Due to the military exercises of the three nations, the sound of gunfire was like firecrackers in Qinhuangdao, and the atmosphere was tense. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Two British submarines and one cruiser stationed in Qinhuangdao left port on the 9th for Weihaiwei. Currently, two British submarines and one cruiser are docked in that port. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The 15th Regiment of American troops stationed in Tianjin, consisting of 240 soldiers, 34 horses, two cannons, and twelve machine guns, boarded a North Ning Railway train this morning at 8:00 AM and departed for Qinhuangdao. They will conduct field exercises in the Yuguan area on the 15th, lasting a total of three days. They also plan to march to the Great Wall line. The second British military exercise in Qinhuangdao has not been scheduled yet and will be held after the French troops' exercise. More troops will participate than in the previous exercise, and detachments from the Tianjin and Beijing garrisons will be sent. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) A certain important figure stated that the British, American, and French barracks in Yuguan are all referred to as fort command posts. Combat exercises have been held annually without notifying any party. The British barracks' rear wall is the Great Wall, and the area outside the wall is designated as a pseudo-border. British soldiers often go outside the city wall for target practice, and it is unreasonable to prohibit them from doing so today. Various countries are quite indignant about this. Therefore, sentries are stationed in front of each barracks, and security is very tight. Furthermore, Japanese soldiers are prohibited from passing through. American and French troops will also conduct exercises, following the usual practice of not notifying. This action is based on the Boxer Protocol, and the Japanese side can do nothing about it. (10th Special Dispatch)

Huang Fu's Trip to Lushan

To Return North Soon to Resume Post

Huang Expected to Arrive at Kuling Last Night

Wang and Chiang Have Already Met Once

(Beiping) Huang Fu telegraphed Beiping on the 9th, stating that he would arrive in Beiping by the end of the month. It is reported that after Huang's trip to Lushan, he will return north via the Jinpu Railway to meet with Han Fuju, Yu Xuezhong, and others. Yin Tong is expected to accompany Huang north to resume his post. (10th Special Dispatch)

Kuling Huang Fu arrived at Xun by Zhongshan warship from the west on the 9th and is expected to arrive at Xun around 7:00 PM on the 10th. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek sent Huang Jinjun, Director of the General Affairs Office of the Military Headquarters, to meet him. He will climb the mountain that evening and arrive at Kuling at 10:00 PM. It is reported that after meeting with Chiang and Wang, Huang will go to Beiping to preside over North China political affairs. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Kuling Huang Fu came west from Nanjing on the Zhongshan warship and is expected to arrive on the 10th evening. He will only stay in Kuling for two or three days. (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Kuling After President Wang arrived at Kuling, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Yang Yongtai, Xiong Shihui, and others went to Wang's residence for talks, leaving after about an hour. Wang decided to go to Haihui Temple at 5:00 AM on the 10th to address the officer corps and return to Kuling that evening. According to Wang's remarks to the Central News Agency reporter at 8:00 PM on the 9th, he came at Chiang's invitation to give a speech to the officer corps and had no other mission. However, since he was already here, he would take the opportunity to discuss central government affairs with Chiang. As for what was discussed, he would disclose it later. (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) It was previously reported that Ambassadors Gu Weijun and Yan Huiqing would go to Lushan to lecture the officer corps on diplomacy. It is now known that there are no preparations for the trip. It is likely that Ambassadors Yan and Gu will prepare to return to their posts, or they may go to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for consultations. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang suggested that provincial and department offices merge and work together, and that this be tried first in the five bandit suppression provinces. If successful, it would be promoted further. It is reported that President Wang also quite agrees. He will have detailed discussions with Chairman Chiang during this trip to Jiangxi, and it will be submitted for discussion at the Fifth National Congress for implementation. (10th Special Dispatch)

Yin Rugeng

Goes to Tianjin to Meet Yu Xuezhong

Chai Shan Has Returned to Beiping from Tanggu

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng is going to Tianjin today to meet with Yu. He will return to Beiping in about a week and then go with Chai Shan to Malanyu to handle the handover with the Japanese representative Mamiya. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong stated that the date for the handover of Malanyu has not been determined because Yin Rugeng has not yet reported. The funds for the Qing Tombs Preservation Committee organized by our side will be paid from the land rent of the tomb area. The preservation committee will create a budget, estimating that it can generate 7,000 yuan per year, which will be sufficient for all expenses. The tomb-guarding police will be limited to 30 men and will not be increased in order to save expenses. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The handover of Malanyu has not been determined because Chai Shan has not yet received a response from the Kwantung Army headquarters, which is why Yin Rugeng has not yet come to Tianjin to ask for instructions on the management plan after the handover. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Chai Shan went to Tanggu last night to pick up his family and arrived in Beiping this morning by the Ping Shen train. According to him, the British and Japanese troops in Yuguan have stopped their exercises. Commander Imamura of the Overseas Fleet came to Tianjin from Lushun but did not go to Yuguan. The issue of the war zone will be actively pursued after Huang Fu and Yin Tong go north, and the seven pending cases discussed in Dalian will be resolved separately. I have not gone to Malanyu for a long time to handle the handover. Dongfang will first hand over Duolun. There is talk of replacing Japanese Ambassador Ariyoshi Akira, but I have not heard of it. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Ping Shen Train Service

Delayed Arrival in Beiping Yesterday

(Beiping) The Ping Shen train, which arrived in Beiping at 9:18 this morning, was delayed by 40 minutes. It is reported that when passing through Beidaihe, the coupling between the North Ning locomotive and the South Manchuria Railway carriage became detached due to uneven height, causing a 40-minute delay. Bandit activity is rampant between Liushouying and Beidaihe on the North Ning Railway. Each passenger train on the North Ning Ping Shen line has been assigned dozens of security guards to protect it.

The Issue of Special Police Deployment to Eastern Hebei

Negotiations Temporarily Stalled

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong stated that the issue of deploying special police to eastern Hebei has been shelved. The Japanese side is most opposed to the proposed number of 9,000 personnel. It may be possible to manage with 6,000 personnel, and light machine guns will not be regarded as heavy weapons. However, this can only be decided after Chairman Huang returns. Our side believes that since the dispute has not been thoroughly resolved, it would be difficult to avoid restrictions if the deployment proceeds rashly. Therefore, it is not currently being actively pursued. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Bali Tai Incident in Tianjin

(Tianjin) The directors of Guangrentang, which owns the land in Nan Kai Bali Tai, Tianjin, are of mixed quality. The director in charge of leasing land to the Japanese is Cai Detang. Other directors believe that Cai's behavior is wrong, and Wang Wendian, a standing committee member of the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce, is most strongly opposed to Cai. Recently, Wang has received multiple anonymous letters, warning that if he does not change his attitude, he will be treated with pistols and bombs. Wang is discouraged by this. Due to rain today, the Japanese side has suspended construction work in Bali Tai for one day. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Panchen Lama Leaves Beiping Today

(Beiping) The Panchen Lama stated that he will go to Suiyuan and Baotou tomorrow, then to Yimeng to chant sutras. He will leave Yimeng at the end of September for Xiangde in Qinghai. The date of return to Tibet will be decided temporarily after arriving in Qinghai. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Xing Sa Ban Zhida arrived in Beiping this morning to visit the Panchen Lama, then entered Mongolia to escort him to Qinghai in the future. The Panchen Lama will leave Beiping tomorrow morning. The Panchen Lama has ordered 20 new cars, which are scheduled to be loaded onto trains tonight. All attendants are also scheduled to board the train tonight. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Belgian Government

Confers Medal on Yu Xuezhong

(Tianjin) At 6:00 PM on the 10th, Hebei Chairman Yu Xuezhong accepted the First Class Grand Cordon of the Order of Leopold conferred by the Belgian Minister. Belgian Minister de Gielgud came to Tianjin this afternoon for the ceremony, which was held at the Belgian Consulate General in the French Concession. More than 40 dignitaries from Hebei Province and Tianjin City, as well as Belgian expatriates and foreign guests, attended. The ceremony was very simple. The Tianjin Consul General Schaer delivered a speech, and Yu Xuezhong responded. Then, the Belgian Minister attached the medal to Yu's sash, and they took a photo together before dispersing. After the ceremony, the Belgian Minister left Tianjin by night train to escape the summer heat in Beidaihe.

(Beiping) Belgian Minister de Gielgud went to Tianjin this morning to preside over the awarding ceremony for Yu Xuezhong. After the ceremony, he went to Beidaihe to escape the summer heat and is expected to return to Beiping at the end of the month. He will go to Tianjin again on the 10th of next month to welcome the Belgian special envoy to China, Johnson, who has already left Brussels and is coming to China via Siberia. He will arrive in Tianjin by boat from Vladivostok in early next month, arrive in Beiping on the 13th, and go to Beijing on the 16th to meet Chairman Lin. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Belgian government awarded Yu Xuezhong the Grand Cordon of the Order of Leopold II. The awarding ceremony was held at the Belgian Consulate at 6:00 PM on the afternoon of the 10th. Belgian Minister de Gielgud came to Tianjin on the morning of the 10th to represent the King of Belgium in awarding the medal. Yu arrived on time with his secretary, wearing a Zhongshan suit. The Belgian Minister welcomed him into the hall and pinned the medal on Yu's chest. Yu expressed his gratitude accordingly. Then, the Belgian Consul General Schaer gave a congratulatory speech, followed by Yu's response. Finally, Chinese and foreign guests applauded to congratulate him. The ceremony concluded around 7:00 PM. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

The German Minister in Beijing

Memorial Service for the Late Hindenburg

(Nanjing) German Minister Trautmann and Rong Kai, the representative of the German legation in Beijing, held a memorial service for the late German President Field Marshal Hindenburg at the Quaker Church in Mercy Lane at 10:00 AM on the 10th. The hall was filled with bamboo and wreaths presented by various circles, which was extremely solemn. Participants included Ye Chucang, representative of our Chairman Lin, Chu Minyi, representative of President Wang, Zhu Hezhong, representative of the Legislative Yuan, Wu Kunwu, representative of the Judicial Yuan, Cheng Zushao, representative of the Control Yuan, Tang Shengzhi and Cao Haosen, representatives of the Military Commission, Xu Mo, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, Wang Shijie, Minister of Education, Luo Wengan, Minister of Justice Administration, Zhu Jiahua, Minister of Communications, He Yaozu, Vice Chief of Staff, and Lin Xiang, Minister of Personnel Affairs, as well as representatives of various foreign embassies and consulates in Beijing and German expatriates in Beijing, totaling about 200 people. At 10:00 AM, the German Minister led the German pastor Wasselew into the hall to ascend the altar. After the entire congregation sang hymns, Pastor Wasselew recited poems and read scriptures. The service lasted for an hour before the meeting was adjourned. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Chu Minyi left Beijing by private car for Moyu Mountain at 11:00 AM on the 10th after attending the memorial service for the late German President on behalf of President Wang in the morning, to handle private affairs. He is expected to return to Beijing around the 12th. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Zhang Yunrong Arrives in Zhangjiakou to Meet Song

(Beiping) Zhangjiakou Telegram: Zhang Yunrong arrived in Zhangjiakou from Gongjigou on the 9th to meet Song and report on the training of Yang Monkey's group. Song plans to go to Zhangbei for inspection within days, or to give a speech to Li's regiment along the way. (10th Special Dispatch)

Communist Bandit Headquarters in Northern Fujian Retreats

剿匪 [Suppression of Bandits] Troops Concentrated at 口口

Will Take Advantage of the Victory to Attack Changting

(Hong Kong) Jiang Dingwen telegraphed Guangdong, saying that the communist bandit headquarters in northern Fujian had retreated. Li Yannian, Liu Kan, and Song Xilian's divisions are all blocking and attacking the remnants of the bandits in the □□□□ area. They are determined to take advantage of the victory to attack Changting. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Huang Tiehan, Commander of the 32nd Central Army, arrived in the province on the 10th to meet with Chen Jitang to discuss coordinating the suppression of bandits in Jiangxi. Yu Hanmou stayed in the province to meet with Sun Ke and extended his leave before returning to his post. Li Yangjing arrived in Huiyang on the evening of the 9th and took a car to Shantou at noon on the 10th. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Jiang Dingwen, Commander-in-Chief of the Eastern Route of the Five Provinces Bandit Suppression Army, telegraphed the military headquarters, saying that the Red Bandits in Gutian and Youxi have been cut into two sections by our army's encirclement. The ends can no longer be connected, and it will not be difficult to eliminate them. According to intelligence reports, the bandits lack both food and weapons and are finding it difficult to sustain themselves. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A certain military agency received a report that the Red Bandits are showing signs of abandoning Changting and fleeing to Ruijin. Once Changting falls, bandit suppression will not be a problem. The bandits are fearful of government troops and dare not engage in battle. Kong Hechong reported four main reasons for the decline of bandit forces, and the total collapse is not far away. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Wang Jingjiu convened a press conference on the 9th and reported five main points: 1. The bandits are adopting guerrilla tactics, aiming to loot salt and rice; 2. The bandits have limited strength, with only about a thousand firearms; 3. Our shortcomings lie in the lack of organization among the people; 4. Fuzhou City is definitely not in danger, and I can guarantee this with my life; 5. Military news should not pick up rumors. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) According to military information, there are currently no bandit traces in Huangtian, Gukou, and other places. Most of the bandits, about 4,000 to 5,000 people, have retreated to the border between Youxi, Datian, Yongde, with only half of them carrying firearms. Their combat strength is very weak. They have been burning, killing, and looting along the way, and colluding with local bandits as guides. The garrisons in the various counties are closely encircling them. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Yesterday, several hundred bandits with broadswords were discovered at Dafu Ridge. After our army's sudden attack, over a hundred bandits were killed. Subsequently, the air force dropped over thirty bombs, killing many bandits. After midnight, the bandits fled to Lotus Mountain via Mo Ling and Ma'an Mountain. Our army is vigorously searching and suppressing them. On the morning of the 9th, the air force had already flown out for reconnaissance. Chen Zhaoying has been focusing on party affairs in the rear and has postponed his trip to Xiamen. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Changsha) According to reports, the remnants of Xiao Ke's bandits have invaded Shang Qidiao Fort in Suichuan. After being severely attacked by our army, they fled towards the Upper and Lower Yuanshan valleys. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Since recovering Guifengtai and Xia Ziling north of Shicheng after passing through Baishui Town, Wang Zhonglian's division has been advancing south step by step. On the 6th, they encountered the bandits' 3rd Army Corps, 4th, 5th, and 6th Divisions at Guanqiao. The bandits occupied important mountain tops, and after a day-long fierce battle, they were finally defeated by the bandits. It is claimed that 400 to 500 bandits were captured, and the division is still following up. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Yellow River Raging

The Situation of River Works in Shandong Suddenly Tense

(Jinan) The River Bureau received a telegram from the Wen County hydrological station in Shaanxi, stating that the Yellow River rose by 1.73 meters at noon on the 9th, with a flow rate of 6,500 cubic meters. On the 10th, it rose again by 1.11 meters, with a flow rate of 8,000 cubic meters. The raging flow is expected to reach Shandong early on the 12th. Due to the sudden tightening of the situation of river works, the River Bureau immediately telegraphed all sections of the river to take strict precautions, and also telegraphed the county chiefs along the river to send personnel to the worksites, urge the mobilization of laborers, and carefully assist. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) The Construction Department sent personnel to survey the entire embankment and design the diversion of the river water to supply the Northern Army River for navigation. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) The Yellow River water level in Wen County was 295.13 meters at Chen hour on the 10th. The river water in Shandong Province is still stable today. The Yellow River Commission telegraphed the River Bureau that Tongguan rose by 9 inches on the 9th, with a water level of 322.95 meters and a flow rate of 6960 meters. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) The Jing and Luo tributaries of the Yellow River in Shaanxi Province rose sharply. On the 10th, the Yellow River in Tongguan rose by 1.6 meters, and the Yellow River in Shaanxi Prefecture rose by 2 meters. (10th Special Dispatch)

Various Counties in Southern Hebei

Drought Followed by Flooding

(Tianjin) After the drought in various counties in southern Hebei, flooding followed. The floodwaters in each county were several feet deep, and the crops were all washed away. Grain prices in dozens of counties such as Longping have increased several times. A dou of millet has increased from 3 jiao to 6 jiao 5 fen, and a dou of red grain has increased from 2 jiao to 4 jiao 1 fen. The people are all suffering endlessly. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Due to the recent heavy rains in North China, the Executive Yuan Administrative Reorganization Committee believes that floods have occurred in various places, which has greatly affected the national economy and people's livelihood. On the 10th, it ordered the investigation department to separately investigate and report the details of the disaster. In the future, it plans to report to the central government based on the investigation results to coordinate relief efforts. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Plague Rampant Outside the Pass

(Beiping) According to intelligence from outside the pass, the plague in the Tongliao area of northern Liaoning and the eastern part of Jilin is still rampant. The Japanese side is only conducting vaccinations in Changchun, Shenyang, and other places, and strictly prohibits merchants and residents from entering Shenyang from the Datong Line and Dahushan to Tongliao, resulting in a large number of plague deaths. According to the death toll announced by the Japanese side, in the area bordering northern Liaoning and Mongolia, 37 people died and 10 people were infected on the 27th of last month. On the 28th, 25 people died and 12 people were infected in Tongliao County alone. By the 31st of last month, a total of more than 60 people had died in the Nong'an area of Jilin. A total of more than 90 people died in Gaojiadian and Yangshulin. Currently, Changchun has implemented epidemic prevention measures, and people from the affected areas have been strictly prohibited from entering the area since the 30th. (10th Special Dispatch)

Bandits Rampant in Various Places in Eastern Luan

(Tianjin) Bandit activity is rampant in various places in eastern Luan. There are large groups of more than a hundred people and small groups of dozens of people, and robbery cases are frequent, especially in the four suburbs of Yuguan. The provincial government recently telegraphed the security forces in the war zone to take responsibility for earnestly suppressing the bandits. More than a hundred bandits from the pseudo-country are gathering at Yiyuan Pass on the Great Wall, intending to enter the country to loot. The militia in Qian'an and Zunhua have stepped up their defenses. Over a hundred police officers from the special public security bureau of the customs clearance area have recently been stationed in Yuguan through negotiations between the bureau chief Su Yuqi and the chief of the Japanese special service agency, Iwai. Iwai has agreed to fully equip them with firearms. Su has telegraphed the provincial government to quickly issue them so that they can defend the area. The provincial government replied that it could allocate 70 to 80 rifles and some ammunition because it did not have pistols. The Japanese side has not yet agreed to the police being equipped with rifles. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Bandit activity has been rampant recently between Liushouying and Beidaihe in the Luan Yu area. The security forces in the Luan Yu area are currently suppressing them separately. In order to protect travelers, the railway bureau has, starting today, strengthened security on trains traveling through that area, in addition to the police escorting the train. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Labor Community of Nanchang

Requests to Suppress Rice Prices

(Nanchang) After two months of severe drought, the heat has returned to 104 degrees Fahrenheit. Due to the high rice prices, the labor community held a meeting on the 9th. Over 40 labor unions, including dockworkers and garment workers, attended and decided to petition the Executive Headquarters, the Provincial Party Headquarters, and the Provincial Government on the 13th to suppress rice prices. The main points are: 1. Investigate the amount of rice in the city; 2. Determine the maximum rice price, which must not exceed 12 yuan, to prevent hoarding again next year during the period between the depletion of last year's harvest and the new harvest. 3. Secretly investigate rice pests and confiscate the affected rice. Also, Saigon rice has arrived in Xunyang, and the market price is 14 yuan, with no further increase. (10th Special Dispatch)

Drawing Water from the Yellow River into the Huiji River

Does Not Affect the Downstream

(Kaifeng) The Fuyang branch of the Anhui Huai River Guiding Association previously heard that this province had a plan to draw water from the Yellow River into the Huiji River and was concerned that it would affect the downstream. It submitted a detailed statement of the advantages and disadvantages, requesting the authorities of this province to prevent its implementation. According to a person in charge of the Construction Department, the Huiji River project is a partial reorganization of the river channels in this province. The eight water suction pipes installed can draw 240 cubic feet of water per second. In addition to the water required by the Huiji River in Kaifeng, the remaining water is not enough to irrigate even a small portion of the farmland along the Huiji River that needs water. The Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission of the Huai River Guidance Commission has repeatedly sent experts to study it and believes that it will definitely not affect the downstream. The way the Jialu River and other river projects will be carried out is still under study. The design in the future will naturally be discussed with all relevant parties to ensure proper implementation. It will definitely not be done at the expense of the neighbor. The Construction Department has sent this opinion to the association. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Hubei Disaster Relief Committee

Decides on the General Outline of Work Relief

Chiang Orders the Formulation of Flood and Drought Prevention Plans

(Hankou) The Disaster Relief Committee decided on the general outline of work relief. The first step of the plan includes: 1. Dredging ponds, dikes, ditches, and canals in 20 counties including Wuchang; 2. Installing siphon pipes at 10 locations including Wutai Gate, Wufeng Gate, and Zhanggong Dike; 3. Placing water pumps in the suburbs of Wuhan. Work relief offices will be established in each county. The organization of disaster relief workers will be 25 people per platoon and 10 platoons per regiment. The current amount of work relief funds is set at 360,000. The disaster situation is most severe in six counties including Hanyang, Jiayu, Huangpi, Xiaogan, Huangmei, and Guangji, and urgent relief will be issued first. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Chiang telegraphed the Hubei Provincial Government to quickly formulate flood and drought prevention plans for this province within the specified time. In addition to submitting a plan for famine prevention projects, the provincial government also ordered the Construction Department to formulate detailed measures and submit them to Chiang for approval. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The Hubei Disaster Relief and Famine Prevention Committee held its second meeting on the 10th, chaired by Meng Guangpeng. The following important cases were resolved: 1. The work group drafted a general outline of construction and methods for disbursing funds, which were revised and approved; 2. 50,000 each was allocated from the agricultural relief and urgent relief funds for work relief; 3. The director of the finance group is responsible for income and expenditure of funds; 4. (4) (6) (7) The cases of hiring and assigning staff for each group were all approved; 8. Since Jia Shiyi is scheduled to go to Xunyang on official business on the 11th, the duties of the finance group will be temporarily assumed by Xia Fuchu. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Severe Drought and Extreme Heat in Hankou City

(Hankou) The heat wave in Wuhan has increased again in recent days, with temperatures above 103 degrees Fahrenheit. There was lightning at noon on the 10th, but still no rain. One porter each died of heatstroke in the Huashang Street and Guanyin Pavilion areas. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) There has been no rain in Hankou for over a month, and the extreme heat is unprecedented. At 2:00 AM on the 10th, the indoor temperature was still 100 degrees. At 2:00 PM on the 10th, the indoor temperature reached 104 degrees, and the sky was clear with no sign of rain. People are both afraid of the extreme heat and worried about the drought, and the situation is extremely dire. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Tang Shizun's Troops Capture Wanyuan

Most of the Red Bandits Flee Northward to Tongjiang

(Chongqing) The 5th and 6th routes of General Commander Tang Shizun captured Wanyuan on the 7th. Most of the Red Bandits fled northward to Tongjiang. According to captured bandit generals, Xu Xiangqian was killed in battle and his body was moved to Hancheng. The remaining bandits are commanded by Zhang Guoshou and Chen Changhao. The Red Bandits still have 60,000 to 70,000 troops concentrated and deployed, intending to break through at one point. (10th Special Dispatch)

Current Commentary

The Austrian Restoration Issue Remains

For the past ten days, the issue of Austrian restoration has once again become a topic of much noise. The Austrian authorities have openly declared that the solution to the Austrian problem must be sought within the Habsburg imperial family, making their intention to restore the monarchy clearly visible. According to European dispatches, Italy's attitude towards this issue also indicates active assistance. Archduke Otto, residing in Belgium, is also eager to try, and there are rumors of a visit to Rome. Observing these three parties, the Austrian restoration issue seems to have progressed further than in the Dollfuss era.

It goes without saying that the increasingly heated nature of this issue is due to Germany's attitude. However, whether Austria's restoration can stem Germany's eastward advance is a major question. Aside from observing the future evolution of events, it is unlikely that anyone can make a prediction. Judging from historical facts, if the Austrian restoration succeeds, Hitler will suffer a major blow. The Habsburg imperial family has traditionally held great prestige among the Germanic peoples, having historically been their leaders. In the 18th century, the kingdoms and principalities of the Germanic peoples on the east bank of the Rhine numbered no fewer than three hundred, with Austria as their ally. After being ravaged by Napoleon's iron heel, they united into thirty-eight states, forming the German Confederation, with Austria still as the leader. Only after the Austro-Prussian War did its leadership position decline, and the prestige of the Habsburg imperial family in Germany was replaced by the Hohenzollern royal family of Prussia. It seems that the current Austrian and Italian authorities are trying to use the past prestige of the Habsburg royal family to carry out a Germanic national fragmentation movement centered on Austria. Those likely to merge with Austria are Bavaria and other places in southern Germany adjacent to Austria. The Germans in these areas are all Catholics, religiously consistent with Austria. If they can be incorporated into Austria, it would weaken Germany's existing power. Judging from the Nazi Party's oppression of Catholics, once the Habsburg restoration succeeds, the return of southern Germany to Austria is not without possibility. Furthermore, after the Habsburg restoration, it could indirectly induce a German restoration, thereby undermining Hitler's rule in Germany. Thirdly, the Habsburg imperial family's historical tendency does not advocate German unification, so the restoration aims to preserve the separation of Germany and Austria. Observing these three effects, the Austrian restoration can indeed inflict significant blows on Hitler. However, given the current strong desire for great unification among the entire Germanic people, whether the fragmentation movement can achieve its wish remains uncertain.

Furthermore, whether this issue can be realized depends on the efforts of the Austrian and Italian authorities, but the key lies in the attitude of the Little Entente countries. According to the pre-war system, the Austrian imperial family was not only the royal family of Hungary, but also the ruler of all of Czechoslovakia and parts of Yugoslavia and Romania. The current Austrian restoration, is it a simple restoration of Austria, or a restoration of Hungary as well? This is a major question. If the restoration is limited to Austria, the power will not be great, and the threat to the Little Entente will not be great either. If the two countries, according to pre-war methods, jointly recognize a monarch and carry out a restoration, the momentum will be greater, and the Little Entente will inevitably be afraid. Moreover, whether the Habsburg imperial family, before the restoration, can recognize the Treaty of Saint-Germain and the Treaty of Trianon, which disposed of Austro-Hungarian lands, is of great importance. If it does not recognize it beforehand, it will inevitably take the recovery of pre-war lost territories as its mission after the restoration, which would endanger the existence of emerging countries such as Czechoslovakia, Romania, and Yugoslavia. Therefore, the Austrian restoration issue must take the Habsburg imperial family's recognition of the above two treaties as a prerequisite, otherwise it will inevitably be opposed by the Little Entente, which will then affect France's attitude. Judging from recent European dispatches, France and the Little Entente are both expressing opposition to this matter, so Italy's attitude has also suddenly turned negative. From this, it can be seen that although this issue has become widely known, whether it can become a reality is still an unknown number.

Six Economic Agreements Signed Between Poland and Danzig

Danzig: Today, Danzig and Poland signed six economic agreements here, reducing tariff and quota restrictions and removing trade barriers between the Free City and Poland. Each agreement will take effect today and will be valid for two years. (10th National Telegram)

Jamaica Boycotts Japanese Goods

Kingston, British Jamaica, will also boycott the dumping of Japanese goods. The local authorities decided today to submit a bill to the Legislative Council when it meets in the autumn to increase import duties on certain foreign manufactured goods. Ironware and cement are also included, with the aim of weakening the competitiveness of Japanese goods against British imports. (9th Reuters)

Roosevelt's Silver Policy

Aimed at stabilizing prices and protecting foreign trade

Nationalization of silver is very helpful in adjusting the value of the currency

Aiming to achieve a three-to-one silver-to-gold ratio in monetary reserves

Abroad, it has caused fears of U.S. currency inflation

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau told reporters today, explaining President Roosevelt's executive order on the nationalization of silver, that the government's move was merely exercising its right of eminent domain. Stock exchange sources said the government wants to actively implement a silver purchase program to respond to calls for inflation. Thomas, the leader of the silver faction, welcomed this announcement, saying that the world's gold-using countries could be overthrown as a result, and a new monetary system and an era of new prosperity would begin from now on. The United States has decided to use more silver coins, which will encourage other countries to adopt the same policy. The U.S. government still needs to buy 1 billion ounces of silver to meet the ratio set by Congress. This order directly declares that the world does not have enough gold to meet currency needs, so it has to turn to silver. (9th Reuters)

Proclamation of Silver Nationalization

President Roosevelt's proclamation on the nationalization of silver states that the U.S. policy is to increase the ratio of silver to gold in U.S. monetary reserves in order to achieve the ultimate goal of a three-to-one silver-to-gold ratio in monetary reserves. The Treasury Department will maintain a 100% silver reserve for the silver certificates it issues. Silver certificates and legal tender for public and private use can be exchanged for standard U.S. dollars upon request. All silver must be delivered to the mint within ninety days, except for domestic and foreign silver coins and ingots, silver owned by foreign governments and foreign central banks, and silver in metal composite products. In the preamble to his proclamation, President Roosevelt said that it is now necessary to seek to increase and stabilize domestic prices and protect U.S. foreign trade to counteract the adverse effects of foreign currency depreciation. (9th Reuters)

U.S. Treasury Secretary Issues Statement

(Washington) The United States suddenly nationalized silver at a price of 50.01 cents per ounce. President Roosevelt ordered the implementation of this this morning under Section 7 of the Silver Act. Tonight, the whole world is paying attention to the Treasury Department's subsequent actions. Various parties have been inquiring with the Treasury Department for the truth. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau has not made any statements, so outsiders can only speculate on their own as to whether this move by the government will have an inflationary effect. According to the Treasury Secretary's statement to the press, a few points are quite important:

(1) The 50% silver transaction profit tax stipulated by the Silver Act is now exempt when silver is nationalized and delivered to the mint.

(2) The price of raw silver remains at 64.5 cents per ounce.

(3) The price of the new currency will be determined based on the price purchased after nationalization, but the Treasury Department will set the price of silver at US$1.2929 per ounce.

(4) Regulations for short-term sales and forward transactions will be announced within a few days.

It is said that this plan was completed a few days ago, but the Treasury Secretary suddenly implemented it this morning. Before issuing the order, the Treasury Secretary telephoned President Roosevelt in Green Bay to ask for instructions, which was approved. (9th National Telegram)

Congressional Silver Faction Satisfied

(Washington) Congressional leaders today all endorsed President Roosevelt's order nationalizing silver. Senators and representatives who were active on currency issues in the last session of Congress said that this move is not an inflationary policy. Democratic Senator Fuller, who is the chairman of the Senate Banking and Currency Committee, said that the nationalization of silver will slightly inflate the currency. He believes that this move can increase both prices and securities prices. Senator Thomas, the leader of the inflation faction, further said that this move is a necessary path for the government to implement the policies set by Congress. Thomas said that this move by the President will have a great impact and will be of great assistance in adjusting U.S. currency policy and the value of the U.S. dollar. (9th National Telegram)

U.S. Senator Borah of Idaho gave a speech here today, advocating that the government establish a central bank to control the national currency. Borah was the leader of the silver faction during the last session of Congress. (9th National Telegram)

Differing Interpretations from Various Parties

(New York) President Roosevelt's executive order today to nationalize silver at a price of 50.01 cents per ounce has been interpreted differently by various parties. The silver faction believes that this move can increase purchasing power in the Far East, but others say that increasing the purchasing power of silver coins will have a contractionary effect in Eastern countries. It is expected that open silver market transactions in the United States will be temporarily suspended as a result. After the order was issued, there was a large-scale sell-off today. Financial circles said that this move by the government indicates its intention to more actively implement the silver policies contained in the Silver Act of 1934. According to general opinion, the U.S. Treasury Department will temporarily purchase more silver, and world silver prices will also rise, because foreign markets will see active buying. (9th Reuters)

Preparation for Possible Inflation

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued an order to implement the Silver Act, nationalizing silver. According to political circles, Roosevelt's decision focuses on achieving psychological effects, because even if the actual silver reserve increases as a result, it will not immediately reach 25%. However, Roosevelt decided to exercise the power given to him by the Silver Act, so that the inflation faction could be partially satisfied, because most senators from agricultural areas are inflationists, who believe that the U.S. dollar has not been sufficiently devalued and want to legally complete the price of the U.S. dollar at 50 cents, according to the amendment proposed by Thomas. But the general public believes that Roosevelt will not immediately enter the path of inflation. This order is just a trial of the situation, and its effect will certainly not be as great as expected by some inflationists. (9th Havas)

(London) The London Financial Times said today that President Roosevelt's opinion on the U.S. dollar is still kept secret, but his silver policy is indeed a preparation for future inflation. The most important impact of President Roosevelt's silver announcement is that foreign observers are concerned that the United States will continue to take inflationary actions. Now it is felt that their concerns are not unfounded. The Daily Mail also said that this U.S. policy is indeed a kind of inflation, but its scope has not reached a very large or alarming degree. However, the Exchange Telegraph said that London operators do not hold the view that this order by the United States is a sign of a new inflationary move. (10th Reuters)

World Markets Fluctuate

(Washington) President Roosevelt's order to nationalize silver had repercussions around the world today, and Washington officials are silently observing its impact. The official arena continuously received reports of disturbances from London, Mumbai, Shanghai, and other important silver markets, but did not issue any opinions. A London telegram reported that China was selling off in large quantities, exceeding the number purchased by London from India. Therefore, London brokers said that if the United States does not assist the market, silver prices will tend to fall. The fluctuations in Mumbai were very large, buying interest was very strong, silver prices soared, and there is a tendency to continue to rise. Silver mining stocks on the London Stock Exchange rose sixpence. New York merchants, however, considered this insignificant and said that its inflationary power will soon disappear. (10th National Telegram)

How Much Silver is Being Purchased is Unknown

(Washington) How much silver the U.S. Treasury Department has recently purchased in the world market is unknown to outsiders. According to estimates, it is about 100 million ounces, and the Treasury Department has also received about 26 million ounces of silver from other sources. Today, Treasury Department personnel claimed that this new order could allow the Treasury Department to purchase at least another 45 million ounces. (9th Reuters)

(London) This morning, people in the London silver market asked each other, "Will the United States buy silver here?" When the news of the United States buying silver was announced, many people in the silver industry were pleased and estimated that the United States had silver reserves ranging from 100 million to 300 million ounces. However, in any case, if the United States wants to implement its silver program, it needs about 1.3 billion ounces of silver. Therefore, many people believe that the United States will inevitably buy silver abroad, in which case silver prices will inevitably rise. However, some people in the silver industry also said that the U.S. government has limited people in the country to hand over their silver reserves within 50 days, so the United States may not purchase in large quantities before November. The news that President Roosevelt has decided to nationalize silver did not have a direct impact, but the indirect impact was the weakness of the U.S. dollar, the popularity of gold mining stocks, and the rise in the prices of goods, because it is feared that there will be a devaluation of the currency after the nationalization of silver. The general opinion is that the greatest impact is the awakening of the psychology of inflation. (10th Reuters)

New York Silver Trading Suspended

(Washington) After the government announced this news, the commodities market immediately suspended trading in silver futures. The silver price at the mint was set at 50.001 cents, which will deduct the minting tax of 61 and 25/8%, and then give the silver owner silver certificates or other currency. This order does not apply to domestically mined silver after December 21 of last year, because this silver can still be sent to the mint in accordance with President Roosevelt's proclamation of December 21. (9th Reuters)

French Monetary Policy Remains Unshaken

(Paris) The French official arena did not express surprise at the U.S. nationalization of silver. The general public believes that this move will not hinder the current policies of the gold bloc countries. Therefore, French financial policy and current international settlement methods will not be inconvenienced. The silver nationalization policy may not be another step for U.S. President Roosevelt to lower the price of the U.S. dollar. Moreover, the amount of silver France stores in the United States is extremely small. Therefore, it can be determined that the U.S. silver nationalization policy will not have an impact in France. (10th Havas)

U.S. Mining Industry Still Unprofitable

Reno, silver mining industry people in Nevada, USA, expressed the opinion that the nationalization of silver has not had a good impact on the Nevada silver industry, because the set price is lower than the price of newly mined silver announced last December. As far as is currently known, Nevada does not store physical silver. Today, the secretary of the Nevada Miners' Association told a Reuters reporter that President Roosevelt's announcement has given the Silver Miners' Association the recognition it wanted. Nevada miners hope that the silver price will be 80 cents or more per ounce, because only at this price can the exploitation of low-grade silver mines be profitable. Currently, this type of silver mine has stopped working. (9th Reuters)

Japan Not Greatly Affected

(Nanjing) Vice Minister of Finance Tsushima spoke as follows regarding U.S. President Roosevelt's announced nationalization of silver:

The purpose of silver nationalization is to increase the value of silver and, due to the demands of inflationists, to be a currency reserve. Also, due to various circumstances such as the recent poor economic situation and the approaching election of councilors, silver nationalization was announced. However, the impact on Japan is not great. However, if the United States implements an inflationary policy, the value of gold may be forced down to an extreme, so changes in its currency system should be noted. (10th Dempo)

Bank of England

Highest Record of Banknote Issuance

Significant Reflection of Business Recovery

(London) The Bank of England's banknote issuing department exceeded £392 million in the week ending August 8, which is the highest record ever. The increase in the amount of banknotes issued was due to holiday needs. This can be regarded as a clear sign of the increase in the spending power of the British people. The London Times said today that the above figures are a significant reflection of the British business recovery. (10th Reuters)

Roosevelt's Speech

Continuing to Promote the New Deal

Increasing Wealth Through Cooperative Action

Seeking the Happiness of the People of the Country

Green Bay: On his way back from touring Hawaii, President Roosevelt delivered his first important speech today, forcefully saying that the government has decided to proceed with its current plans, and that in terms of finance, the government is implementing its "golden rule." Those protected by the government are not only homeowners who are free from the danger of enclosed properties, but also small property owners, depositors, and investors, who can now rest easy. When the President spoke of the people's gradual restoration of confidence in the New Deal, he cited agricultural programs, the industrial programs of the National Recovery Administration, and the government's relief programs, and recognized that they were sufficient to restore the nation's belief and courage. The President also said that the New Deal, which cracks down on harming others for one's own benefit, will continue to be promoted, but said that the government does not want to hinder honest commerce, nor does it intend to take from one and give to the other. The government's sole purpose is to increase wealth through cooperative action and to share it with the people of the country. (9th National News Agency)

Some members of the mission also drove Italian aircraft for distance test flights. The observation mission was very interested in the experimental work of the Montecelio Airfield and was especially grateful for the enthusiasm of the Italian reception. Russian Flight Team

Warmly Welcomed by France and Italy

Banquet Visits Every Day

(Paris) Today at noon, the Military Club hosted a banquet for the Soviet Russian aviators who arrived here yesterday, presided over by Minister of Aviation General Denain. French officials, both civil and military, who accompanied the seat included representatives from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and officers and technicians who had accompanied former Minister of Aviation Cot to the Soviet Union last year. At the end of the banquet, General Denain addressed the guests, first explaining the relationship between the Russian and French aviation circles, and then saying that the Russian aviation circles had ascended to the stratosphere and made various famous flights, which were admirable. Admiral Osumi Criticizes

British and American Naval Claims

Opposes Proportionalism

(Nanjing) Admiral Osumi went to the Nasu Imperial Villa on the 9th to meet with the Emperor and reported on the naval situation. After that, he returned to Tokyo in the same car with Prime Minister Okada. On the issue of arms reduction in the car, the Admiral said that Prime Minister Okada had stated that he opposed proportionalism, and that he held the same opinion. U.S. Admiral Pratt argued for proportionalism on the grounds that Japan is only located on one shore in the Orient, while the United States is between the Atlantic and Pacific Oceans and has a very long coastline. This kind of argument may be considered reasonable by ordinary people, but from the perspective of experts, it has no practical basis. War is decided when the forces of the two countries meet in one place. It is most important to consider these various occasions and decide on national defense power. The United Kingdom also advocates proportionalism because it has colonies overseas, but if the United Kingdom loses its colonies, it can still recover the lost land if it wins the final battle. Therefore, the problem of protecting overseas colonies can be achieved by maritime police. Their advocacy of proportionalism is nothing more than wanting to maintain a naval force larger than other countries. The purpose of arms reduction conferences can only be achieved if the largest military power sacrifices the most military equipment. (10th Domei)

Page 8

The Japanese Foreign Ministry and the Military

Contending for Supervisory Power over the Puppet Regime

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of unifying and strengthening the resident organs in Manchuria, negotiations have been conducted by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Army, the Colonization Ministry, and related ministries, and there is a growing trend towards concrete progress. The Army's intention is that this reform of the organs should first determine its fundamental principles. Therefore, the fundamental methods of its reform plan are roughly as follows:

1. The roots of the current resident organs in Manchuria are the Plenipotentiary Ambassador, the Commander of the Army, and the Governor-General of Kwantung. This tripartite system should be changed to a dual system of the Plenipotentiary Ambassador and the Commander of the Army, abolishing the Governor-General of Kwantung. Since the current state of "Manchukuo" has been based on the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol, the primary goal should be joint defense and ensuring public security between Japan and Manchukuo. Therefore, the Commander of the Kwantung Army should concurrently serve as the Plenipotentiary Ambassador. The Plenipotentiary Ambassador should be under the direct supervision of the Prime Minister, but regarding purely diplomatic affairs, he should still be under the supervision of the Minister of Foreign Affairs as before. As for the Commander of the Army, he should be under the supervision of the Minister of the Army regarding items related to commanding military orders and the issue of public security in "Manchukuo".

However, the opinion of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is that regarding the dual system of the Commander of the Army and the Plenipotentiary Ambassador, specifically the Commander of the Army concurrently serving as the Plenipotentiary Ambassador, they do not object. However, regarding the issue of supervisory power, they believe that the Plenipotentiary Ambassador should still be under the command and supervision of the Minister of Foreign Affairs as before. Thus, the authorities of the Army and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are in a mutually conflicting situation regarding fundamental principles. However, if the reform plan resulting from this dual system is decided based on these principles, it would be easy to resolve. If the Army and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs each insist on their own views on the above issues, and fail to reach a consensus on future negotiations, the outcome may be that the Prime Minister, the Foreign Minister, and the Army Minister organize a three-minister meeting, and make a decision based on the policy towards Manchuria and the overall interests of the nation. Indeed, there is no other way. Furthermore, the Army's argument for placing the Plenipotentiary Ambassador under the direct supervision of the Prime Minister is roughly as follows:

(1) The relationship between "Manchukuo" and Japan, based on the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol, has an inseparable special relationship in terms of national defense and diplomacy. At the same time, there is also an inseparable close relationship in terms of industrial development and all other facilities. Therefore, for the sake of the coexistence and co-prosperity of the two countries, it is necessary to provide great assistance. Its diplomatic relations with other countries are completely different. (2) The diplomacy of "Manchukuo" must simultaneously consider Japan's diplomatic policy. The scope of purely diplomatic affairs executed by the Plenipotentiary Ambassador is extremely narrow, and there is a close relationship with the Japanese Ministry of Colonization, Agriculture and Forestry, Commerce and Industry, and Railways in the development of industry, economy, railways, and other various aspects. In these various relationships, placing the Plenipotentiary Ambassador under the supervision of the Prime Minister to unify and strengthen the relationship with Japan is considered appropriate and convenient for the development of "Manchukuo" and the implementation of Japan's policy towards Manchuria.

(3) As for changing the title of the Plenipotentiary Ambassador to the Plenipotentiary Representative in Manchuria, it is believed that the current title is not very appropriate when "Manchukuo" establishes diplomatic relations with other countries in the future. Therefore, the title is being considered this time. If it is considered appropriate, please change it. Otherwise, it is also acceptable to keep the current title of Plenipotentiary Ambassador. (10th day, Japanese United News)

British Industrial Representatives

To Visit the Puppet State for Inspection

Stating it's a Private Action

(London) The Federation of British Industries decided today to send an industrial delegation to "Manchukuo" in the near future to inspect everything and ascertain whether the British industrial sector can fully cooperate with the local industrial sector to develop various businesses. The delegation will also make a short trip to Japan to establish friendly contacts with Japanese industrial and commercial representative groups. The delegation will consist of Sir Barnes, director of Lloyds Bank and Commercial Union Assurance Company, Sir Seligman, director of Seligman Brothers, several bankers, one member of the Advisory Committee of the Export Credits Guarantee Department, Mr. Rogerson, director of the Federation of British Industries, and Mr. Bigood, representative of the British Iron and Steel Federation. Mr. Bigood was born in Japan. (8th day, Reuters)

(London) Government officials today declared regarding the industrial delegation's visit to "Manchukuo" for inspection that the delegation will receive various legitimate assistance from the British government. The delegation is now scheduled to depart at the end of the month to investigate the situation of opening up new markets. It is also heard that the delegation has reported to the government, stating that this trip is purely a private action of a commercial nature. As for whether British private debt lending to "Manchukuo" conflicts with the non-recognition policy passed by the League of Nations, responsible parties stated that the government naturally considers this loan not to be of a political nature, but the Treasury Department has the right to decide on this issue afterwards. (10th day, National News)

(London) The Federation of British Industries has decided to send an industrial inspection delegation to "Manchukuo" in the near future, as reported in the previous telegram. Recently, The Times and the Morning Post have both published commentaries. The Times stated, "The fact that the industrial sector has taken this action shows that they are not unaware that there are new markets to be found in the Far East. We anticipate that after the inspection delegation travels to Japan, they will be able to take the opportunity to inspect major commercial centers in China and establish friendly contacts with leaders in the Chinese business and financial sectors. The main task of the inspection delegation is to examine the extent to which British commerce and finance can assist the development of "Manchukuo". Under the current circumstances, there are various benefits to British banks cooperating with the Japanese. If British and Japanese industrialists can cooperate sincerely, the positive impact will not be limited to "Manchukuo". It is no exaggeration to say that the entire Far East will benefit from it." The Morning Post also had the same opinion, stating, ""Manchukuo" is rich in resources, and its economic development will be very rapid. The British inspection delegation's trip will certainly be welcomed by the emperor and government of "Manchukuo". If this is the case, it will be beneficial to both parties. Furthermore, the inspection delegation will travel from Manchuria to Japan, which shows that our people do not pay much attention to the so-called threat that Japan poses to British commerce, and instead recognize that Anglo-Japanese friendship is the greatest benefit to Britain in the Far East. If Britain and Japan can adopt common solutions to common problems, the friendship between the two countries will be further consolidated. The inspection delegation is heading to the Far East with this spirit, and its future political and economic gains will benefit both countries." (10th day, Havas)

Sino-Soviet Railway Negotiations

Russia Rejects Japanese Proposal

Insisting on Original Claims

(Nanjing) Soviet Ambassador to Japan, Mr. Yurenev, visited Foreign Minister Hirota at 3:30 PM on the 10th, stating briefly that he had received the final compromise proposal for the Sino-Soviet Railway sale negotiations submitted by the Foreign Minister on the 30th of last month, requesting further consideration. He then requested instructions from his home government and received a reply today, stating that the Soviet government still feels that the proposal submitted on the 30th of last month is extremely appropriate and requests that the Foreign Minister convey to "Manchukuo" to make further concessions to bring it closer to the Soviet position, and requests continued mediation. This did not touch on the Foreign Minister's final mediation plan at all. The Foreign Minister said that if his mediation is not accepted, he will resign from his position as mediator and requests direct negotiations with "Manchukuo", which he had stated before. However, the Soviet side still hopes that the Foreign Minister will mediate. Therefore, Foreign Minister Hirota replied in a stern tone, saying that if the Soviet government is unwilling to accept his final compromise plan and is proposing a new plan, he absolutely cannot agree. However, at this time, he still hopes to make concessions to improve the relationship between Japan, Manchukuo, and the Soviet Union. If he still conveys this matter to "Manchukuo" today, he will still insist on the mediation plan in his position as mediator and will strive to the end to uphold the principles expressed in the final proposal. If it is not recognized, there will be no other way but direct negotiations.

In addition, various situations were discussed. From this, it can be seen that the Sino-Soviet Railway sale negotiations are still in a state of back-and-forth. If the Soviet Union continues to maintain its tough attitude, the negotiations may even break down, and its future is quite bleak. (10th day, Japanese United News)

Dissolution of Austrian Social Democratic Stormtroopers

Another Expression of German Compromise Towards Austria

Cabinet to Be Changed Soon

Vice Chancellor Goering Most Likely

Munich The headquarters of the Austrian National Socialist Party here was closed today. This is the second move by German Chancellor Hitler to appease the Austrians. The first move was to ban official sponsorship of anti-Austrian radio propaganda. (9th day, Reuters)

Munich German authorities today issued an order to dissolve the Austrian National Socialist stormtroopers. Upon the issuance of this order, the stormtrooper camps will be dismantled one after another, and all members will be demobilized, which can be completed within a week. This can be regarded as another clear indication of Germany's adoption of a new compromise policy towards Austria. It is also the actual effect of the unanimous condemnation of Germany by world public opinion after the murder of Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss. All parties are therefore optimistic about the future of the European situation. Chancellor Hitler's anger towards France and the open expression of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, although seemingly indifferent, are actually concerned about the increasing backlash from various countries. Therefore, his policy towards Austria is gradually becoming more moderate. The actual number of Austrian National Socialist stormtroopers has not been disclosed to the outside world, but it is known that approximately 15,000 to 20,000 troops are stationed in barracks, mostly on the border between Austria and Bavaria. (10th day, Reuters)

(Berlin) The German cabinet will be changed soon, but the official announcement will likely be made after the referendum on August 19th. The positions of Vice President and Deputy Prime Minister will likely be combined into one, and one person will be appointed to it, titled Deputy Head of the German Federation. Those who are expected to hold this position include Prussian Prime Minister and Minister of Aviation General Goering, Minister of Defense General Blomberg, and media mogul Hugenberg. Among them, General Goering is the most likely, because if General Blomberg holds this position, it will make the National Defense Forces too closely linked to politics. As for Hugenberg's rise to power, many of Hitler's party members regard it as an open victory for the right wing, so they do not approve of it. (9th day, Reuters)

Austrian New Premier Visits Hungary and Romania

Vienna Prime Minister Schuschnigg, accompanied by Minister of Culture Pernter, went to the city of Szeged in Hungary to attend the performance of the Austrian poet Grillparzer's "The Scapegoat", and arrived there tonight. Prime Minister Schuschnigg plans to fly from Szeged to the Hungarian capital tomorrow morning to meet with Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös. According to well-informed sources, Austria and Hungary have a treaty of mutual consultation. This trip by Schuschnigg is to inform the Hungarian Prime Minister of the intentions of the new Austrian government regarding this matter. (9th day, Havas)

Vienna Austrian new Prime Minister Schuschnigg visited the Romanian capital today. People in Vienna have made many speculations about this trip. It is heard that Schuschnigg has discussed various important matters with government officials. (10th day, Reuters)

Our Country's Youth

Walking Around the Globe

A Journey of 24,000 Kilometers

Arriving in London Via the New World

(London) Chinese youth Zhang Zhenying (transliteration), who is walking around the earth, has traveled 24,000 kilometers and has now arrived in London. He departed in 1929, passed through Japan, North America, and northern South America, and arrived in Peru in 1931. He then took the route through Chile, Argentina, and Europe to return to China. However, in South America, he encountered the war between Paraguay and Bolivia, and also encountered a volcanic eruption, almost losing his life. He then crossed the Andes Mountains and plans to return to his hometown of Guangzhou in 1937. (10th day, Havas)

Ministry of Industry Denies

State-Run Shen Xin Textile Factory

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry issued a statement on the handling of the Shen Xin Textile Factory case, stating that the claim of nationalization is baseless rumors. Item 3 of the relief measures proposed by the Ministry, in which the government provides 3 million as operating capital, is specifically for maintaining the Shen Xin business for six months of working capital and does not include debt and has nothing to do with state-run operations. (10th day, Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry instructed the Wuxi Textile Association regarding the handling of the Shen Xin Textile Factory case, stating that the Ministry previously received a report from Rong Zongjing, stating that the company's finances were exhausted and requesting that personnel be sent to investigate and provide prompt relief. The Ministry then immediately formulated a temporary plan: (1) the Executive Yuan should send a letter to the National Economic Commission to maintain the company and prevent it from stopping work; (2) the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry should send a letter to the National Economic Commission to send personnel to jointly investigate and formulate a relief plan to be implemented under government supervision. The Executive Yuan meeting approved and complied, and personnel were immediately sent to jointly investigate with personnel from the National Economic Commission and the Ministry of Finance. They jointly proposed a relief plan for approval. Subsequently, the personnel reported that they had estimated the company's assets and liabilities, and although the liabilities exceeded 5 million yuan, the actual amount that urgently needed to be repaid was more than that. They also submitted a written report for verification. After review, another relief plan was formulated: (1) the government should order the company to liquidate, with a deadline of six months. If liquidation fails, the government will send personnel to liquidate; (2) the government should convene creditors and organize a temporary management committee to operate the company's existing nine factories, with a deadline of six months. After six months, a specific plan will be determined based on the results of the reorganization; (3) during the temporary management committee's operation period, the government will provide 3 million yuan as operating capital. At the end of six months, all profits or losses will be calculated into the company's debt and credit, and submitted to the Executive Yuan meeting for approval. However, because the company sent personnel to reorganize itself, a decision was not made. In summary, the Ministry's handling of this case has been based on the principle of supporting private enterprises, focusing on maintaining both the Shen Xin business and the rights of creditors. The official documents are clear and obvious. The claim of nationalization is entirely baseless rumors. At this time when the domestic textile industry is in danger, it is difficult to guarantee that there are no villains confusing the public. The reporters in this case have experience in handling social affairs and should weigh the facts and remain calm. How can they pick up rumors and make inquiries? As for the estimation of Shen Xin's assets, because the textile industry involves specialized technology, experts sent by the National Economic Commission conducted a detailed estimation during the investigation. According to the report, the estimated value is too low and a letter should be sent to investigate and reply. Also, Item 3 of the relief measures proposed by the Ministry, in which the government provides 3 million yuan as operating capital, is specifically for maintaining Shen Xin's business for six months of working capital and does not include debt, and has nothing to do with state-run operations. This is for your information. (10th day, Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry recently issued a detailed reply to the Wuxi Textile Association's request for relief for the Shen Xin Textile Factory, stating that the Ministry's handling of this case has been based on the principle of supporting private enterprises, focusing on maintaining both the Shen Xin business and the rights of creditors. The claim of nationalization is entirely baseless rumors. (10th day, Central News Agency)

Anhui Drought Tragedy

Farmers Dig Dike to Divert Water for Irrigation

Dike Collapses and Crushes Six Laborers to Death

(Anqing) At the Weijiakou section of the Guangji Dike, more than ten miles away from the province, a dike was dug to divert water for irrigation. At 6:30 AM on the 10th, it suddenly collapsed, crushing six laborers to death. Liu Zhenhua and the heads of various departments went to inspect. It has been a continuous drought without rain for days. The highest temperature was 107 degrees. There have been many deaths due to heatstroke. (10th day, Special Dispatch)

(Anqing) This year's drought has caused a disaster. On the 8th, a rice-snatching riot broke out at Gaohebu, sixty miles away from the city. More than a thousand hungry people gathered and searched house to house. All the stored rice was looted, and the situation is serious. However, there have been no cases of looting of property. (9th day, Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) Here rice rose to thirteen yuan and two corners. In the afternoon of the 10th, there was a heavy rainstorm for two hours. Beiping Political Reorganization Committee

Crack Down on Adulteration of Water in Cotton

(Beiping) According to political sources, in recent years, due to the petty profits gained by a group of unscrupulous merchants, the export of cotton from our country often involves the adulteration of water and other substances, which has often caused dissatisfaction among foreign merchants and has greatly affected foreign trade. Based on the "Provisional Regulations for Cracking Down on Water Adulteration of Cotton" promulgated by the National Government, the Political Reorganization Committee strictly ordered the five provinces and two municipalities to effectively crack down on this. Furthermore, the cotton production in western Hebei has always been abundant, and it can generate profits of 30 million yuan each year. However, due to the adulteration of water by unscrupulous merchants and improper transportation and sales methods, it has plummeted. Recently, the North China Rural Improvement Society, composed of the School of Economics of Nankai University, the Jin Cheng Bank, and the Ding County People's Education Promotion Association, discussed ways to improve cotton at Beiping, and decided to train 60 instructors to specialize in the development of western Hebei cotton. Large warehouses will be built in five counties along the Hutuo River, with complete equipment for compressing and packaging cotton. At the same time, farmers' loans will be offered at an annual interest rate of 8%. In the future, the warehouse will purchase and sell the cotton after the harvest. In addition, 500 mu of land will be allocated in Ding County as a cotton seed experimental area. (10th day, Central News Agency)

Two More Principals Arrested in the Yin Case

(Tianjin) In the case of American missionary Henry Inn, the Wanping County Government has arrested two more principals. They were escorted to the 51st Army Headquarters in Tianjin on the morning of the 10th. A total of eight suspects have been arrested in the case. Yu Xuezhong has telegraphed the Beiping Military Branch to ask for instructions. After receiving a reply, they will be executed. (10th day, Central News Agency)

The Supreme Court's Judgment Revokes the Portion Regarding Deprivation of Civil Rights

Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi Each Sentenced to Eight Years Imprisonment

Beijing News: The Supreme Court announced on the 10th the criminal judgment on the appeal case of Chen Duxiu and others for endangering the Republic. The full text is as follows:

Appellant Chen Duxiu, male, 56 years old, from Huaining County, residing in Yongxing Lane, Yuezhou Road, Shanghai, unemployed. Peng Shuzhi, also known as Zhang Cinan, male, 36 years old, from Baoqing County, residing in Chunyang Lane, Dong Youheng Road, Shanghai, unemployed. Wang Wu, also known as Song Fengchun, male, 27 years old, from Cang County, residing in Liangxi Inn, Sima Road, Shanghai, unemployed. Pu Yifan, male, 29 years old, from Huaining County, working as an editor for the China Merchants Bureau Monthly in Gaofu Lane, Shanghai. Wang Zhaoqun, male, 29 years old, from Su County, residing in Chunyang Lane, Dong Youheng Road, Shanghai, teacher. Guo Jinghao, also known as Peng Daozhi, male, 23 years old, from Baoqing County, studying at Xiude Lane, Baike Road, Shanghai. The above appellants, in a case of endangering the Republic, appealed against the first instance judgment of the Jiangsu High Court on April 26, 1933. This court's judgment is as follows:

Main Text: The original judgment regarding Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi, and the portion of the deprivation of civil rights of Wang Wu, Pu Yifan, Wang Zhaoqun, and Guo Jinghao are all revoked. Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi are each sentenced to eight years of imprisonment for using writing to promote treason.
