Factory Inspection Problems

International Attention to This Issue and Expression of Sympathy

The Social Bureau Sends Personnel Abroad for Observation

According to the Central News Agency, the factory inspection problem in this city has been stalled due to the obstruction of the concession authorities, causing the Chinese-controlled areas to also come to a standstill. However, factory inspection is of great importance to industrial safety, so our country's authorities will seek new methods to resolve it. The following is based on a reporter's inquiry into various situations:

International Sympathy Expressed

The failure to implement factory inspections in this city is indeed due to the failure of the concession authorities to show sincerity, leading to a standstill. At the International Labor Conference, Li Pingheng, Director of the Industrial Department of the Ministry of Industry, presented a report on this matter and explained the reasons why factory inspections should be managed by the Chinese government. Therefore, international attention has been drawn to this matter, and sympathy has been expressed. Currently, our country has also been elected as a permanent director of the conference, and we will certainly strive for justice based on reason in the future. Although the realization of this goal still requires time, it may be possible to break the current stalemate.

The Municipal Social Bureau is Actively Preparing

According to the New Voice News Agency, the factory inspection problem has already been addressed by the Central Factory Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, which has stipulated inspection procedures and distributed them to various provinces and cities for implementation. The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, in view of the dangers of factory boilers, has requested the municipal government to send factory inspector Lu Jicang to the Babcox & Wilcox boiler factory in the United Kingdom for practical training and to inspect foreign factory boiler equipment, so as to serve as a reference for factory inspections in our country. Now Mr. Lu's passport has been processed, and he is scheduled to go abroad at the end of this month. Mr. Lu is a graduate of the Department of Mechanical Engineering of Jiaotong University and is scheduled to practice in the UK for two years and six months.

Ruian County Forced to Acknowledge Highway Share Payment

All Ships Decide to Suspend Service

Due to Unfairness and Inability to Cope

Appeals to the Executive Yuan, Ministries, and Provincial and County Governments

According to the New Voice News Agency, the four shipping companies of Hushing, Daxing, Zhejiang, and Ruian, due to the Ruian County Government's sole responsibility for acknowledging and paying 60,000 yuan of highway share payment assigned by the province, held a meeting yesterday and resolved that if the county government forces the acknowledgment and payment, they will unanimously suspend service in response. The Shipping Industry Association continued to appeal to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Communications, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, the Construction Department, and the Ruian County Government to not force the acknowledgment and payment. The details are as follows:

Emergency Meeting

Ships operating on the Shanghai-Ruian-Pingyang line, including the Xinruiping and Ruiping ships of Hushing Company, the Sanjiang and Fuxing ships of Daxing Company, the Deli ship of Zhejiang Company, and the ships of Ruian Company, are being forced by the Ruian County Government to acknowledge and pay highway share payments assigned by the province, which is scheduled to be implemented on the 16th of this month. Therefore, an emergency meeting was held at 10:00 AM yesterday at the Shipping Club on Guangdong Road, and it was resolved that if Ruian County continues to force the acknowledgment and payment of highway share payments, all ships will unanimously suspend service in response. The meeting adjourned at around 11:00 AM.

Telegram to Ruian County

The Shipping Association telegraphed the Zhejiang Construction Department and the Ruian County Government yesterday, stating that, according to a joint statement from members Hushing Company, Daxing Company, Zhejiang Company, and Ruian Company, the Ruian County Government has assigned the 60,000 yuan of highway share payments assigned by the province solely to the four companies to acknowledge and pay. The company has repeatedly stated the situation and earnestly requested that another method of raising shares be devised, but this has not been approved. However, if the full amount of the highway payment is to be forcibly acknowledged solely by the shipping companies, it will be impossible to comply in reality. In addition to detailing the reasons, we have also sent a separate letter requesting that your association forward it to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Communications, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government, ordering that another method of raising shares be devised so as to avoid a suspension of service being forced to occur and also earnestly requesting your association to telegraph the Construction Department and the Ruian County Government to take note that, before receiving instructions from the Executive Yuan, ministries, and provinces, please do not force our company to pay the share payment so as to avoid accidents and maintain transportation. We are deeply grateful, etc., have been received by the association. In addition to submitting a separate document to the Executive Yuan, ministries, and the provincial government, we hereby telegraphed the situation to request your attention and approval for forwarding instructions to the Ruian County Government for notification. We are most grateful. Yu Hede, Chairman of the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association, respectfully greets you.

Separate Submissions to the Executive Yuan and Ministries

Another document submitted to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Communications, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government stated, "Submitting this document regarding the Ruian County Government's order for shipping companies to solely bear the highway share payments, and elaborating on the difficulty in complying with the actual situation, earnestly request approval to instruct the Zhejiang Provincial Government to instruct another fair method to be devised, so as to maintain the shipping industry. According to a joint statement from members of the Hushing Commercial Shipping Company, Daxing Commercial Shipping Company, Zhejiang Shipping Company, and Ruian Commercial Shipping Company, the Ruian County Government has ordered the four companies to solely acknowledge and pay the full amount of 60,000 yuan of highway share payments assigned by the province. With the current shipping industry declining to an extreme point, it is difficult to comply with the order to solely acknowledge and pay a huge amount of highway share payments. Our company has previously stated the situation to the Ruian County Government, earnestly requesting that another good policy be devised, but this has not been approved. Subsequently, we sent another letter to your association, requesting that it be forwarded to the Construction Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, instructing the Ruian County Government to devise another method to demonstrate fairness. However, the Ruian County Magistrate replied to your association by telegram, still requesting that we be persuaded to acknowledge and pay. Our company sent a previous letter to your association, conveying the situation, and it was a last resort. The method of raising highway share payments should first involve local wealthy individuals and various industries sharing the burden. Shares are solicited in various counties and ports to form a case. There has never been a precedent for solely acknowledging and paying. However, the Ruian County Government has resolutely taken this action, going its own way, and solely ordering the four companies to subscribe to the full amount of the road shares. With the current situation of the four companies, it is impossible to comply in reality. Even considering the circumstances and reasoning, it is extremely unfair. According to the Ruian County Government's telegram to the Construction Department regarding the method of raising shares, the wording is to order each shipping company to restore passenger and freight fares, and use the increased income to acknowledge and pay the road shares. However, it is not known whether the passenger and freight fares should be restored. It is entirely a painful measure during a time of commercial depression. Shipping companies have been affected by the decline in the rural economy in recent years, and their business has been declining to the point of exhaustion. Fortunately, they rely on devaluation to save more passengers and goods, hoping to survive. Observing the current situation, restoring the original price is not yet the time. Moreover, this kind of plan is a measure that each company has no choice but to take. The government is not familiar with the commercial situation and comes out to help plan, saying that the meeting has been passed. At the Ruian County Highway Share Raising Meeting on April 26 of this year, County Magistrate Chen first drafted three proposals: (1) wealthy individuals' share payment, (2) merchants' share payment, and (3) overseas shipping companies' share payment. Because most of the attendees at the time were non-shipping industry people, in order to avoid acknowledging and paying shares, they abandoned the first and second proposals and resolved to adopt the third method of raising share payments from overseas shipping companies. However, the four companies only sent representatives from the Ruian agencies to attend the meeting nearby, and they did not have the right to represent the head office to vote. Therefore, the third item in the meeting minutes recorded that the implementation of this case would be communicated by the Ruian branch of each company to the Shanghai head office, and personnel would be sent to Ruian to make a decision. Therefore, the so-called meeting pass was entirely advocated by people outside the shipping industry. The original intention was to avoid acknowledging and paying shares on their own and to delegate the major responsibility to others. The facts are obvious, and if they want to force the implementation by this, the shipping companies will not willingly endure being deceived by the Construction Department and ordered to comply. The shipping companies have stated the situation, but it has been ignored, resulting in the case being suspended for several months. Our company believes that the crux of this case lies entirely with the Ruian County Magistrate's lack of consideration and improper measures. What is worried is that the county magistrate is still adhering to his established views and will not only not change the original plan but will also force its implementation. Under this situation, our company is panicked and has no way to appeal. We can only request your association to forward the request to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Communications, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government as soon as possible, ordering the county to devise another method of raising share payments, so as to avoid a forced entry by shipping companies and causing inconvenience to transportation in the county. We are deeply grateful, etc." The association replied that the claims were true, so it specially forwarded the request, hoping that it would be reviewed and approved to order the Zhejiang Provincial Government to instruct the Ruian County Government to devise another fair method, so as to maintain the shipping industry. We are waiting for orders.

Rickshaw Pullers' Dispute Unresolved

More than a Hundred Arrested, Each Detained for Several Days and Fined Six Yuan

Concessionaires Petition the Municipal Council, Which Agrees to Strict Protection

Rickshaw Pullers' Representatives Send Letter to the Rickshaw Committee, Denying the Petition

The Public Concession Municipal Council, adopting the recommendations of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee, improved the treatment of rickshaw pullers and stipulated new regulations, reducing rickshaw rental fees. However, due to objections from the rickshaw owners regarding the new regulations, the newly stipulated regulations have not yet been implemented and have been repeatedly postponed. It is now heard that the Municipal Council has decided to implement the new regulations from the 15th of this month, but the rickshaw pullers mistakenly believe that the new regulations have already been implemented. The day before yesterday, when some rickshaw pullers rented rickshaws from the owners, they were only willing to pay the rental fees according to the amount stipulated in the new regulations. The rickshaw owners refused to accept and stopped renting out rickshaws. Because the rickshaw pullers had no rickshaws to pull, their livelihoods were greatly affected, so they went to the Rickshaw Committee to petition. Along the way, they were joined by idle people who were not rickshaw pullers. When they saw rickshaw pullers pulling rickshaws, regardless of whether there were passengers on the rickshaws, they removed the screws from the vehicles, causing the air in the rubber tires to be immediately released. The rickshaw then lost its rolling efficiency and could not be driven. This kind of prank quickly spread throughout the Public Concession, and the number of rickshaw pullers who had no rickshaws to pull and engaged in sabotage also increased with time. The police authorities reported that such behavior not only hindered traffic but also interfered with the freedom of others and affected social order. They immediately ordered the 14 police stations under their jurisdiction to select Chinese and foreign detectives to closely guard their respective areas. If the above-mentioned situation was found, they should be properly dissuaded, and those who resisted should be detained. On one side, Deputy Superintendent McTing and Deputy Chief Detective Lu Dagong went out to investigate. As a result, detectives from each police station were dispatched, and detectives were like shuttles on each road. The removal of screws also occurred repeatedly. In total, from morning to evening the day before yesterday, except for the areas under the jurisdiction of the Huisi and Yangshupu police stations, which did not have any incidents, the total number of rickshaw pullers detained for removing screws or damaging vehicles was 11, including Li Zhengyuan, detained by the General Police Station; 20, including Yuan Shihua, detained by the Old Gate Police Station; 4, including Chen Zhenzi, detained by the New Gate Police Station; 14, including Zhao Daniu, detained by the Chengdu Road Police Station; 2, including Zhou Lihuai, detained by the Pudu Road Police Station; 27, including Pan Xiaoshaozhi, detained by the Jing'an Temple Police Station; 3, including Chen Asan, detained by the Gordon Road Police Station; 9, including Sun Shilin, detained by the Hongkou Police Station; 5, including Zhu Fulu, detained by the Huichu Police Station; 2, including Sun Shouyuan, detained by the Yulin Road Police Station; 5, including Mao Shunqing, detained by the Jiaxing Road Police Station; and 2, including Sun Junru, detained by the Dixiwei Road Police Station, totaling 103 people. All of them were sent to the First Special District Local Court yesterday morning. Because of the large number of people, the two judges Deng Baosun and Huang Risheng opened two courts to interrogate them separately. The Municipal Council was also represented by the two lawyers Jiang Baolian and Qian Xunjiu, who filed a lawsuit against each defendant based on Article 318 of the Criminal Law for obstructing freedom. After Deng and Huang respectively examined the cases, they determined that the defendants should be held responsible for the charges against them, so they immediately announced the verdicts in court. Some were fined, and some were sentenced to detention, based on the severity of the circumstances. The amount of the fine was mostly six yuan per person, and the length of detention was five days or seven days, depending on the case. Those who were unable to pay the fine were also sentenced to detention according to the law.

Letter to the Rickshaw Committee Denies Petition

Yesterday, Chen Guoliang and others, the rickshaw pullers' representatives who attended the Municipal Council in the Special District, sent a letter to Mr. Maxwell of the Rickshaw Committee, stating, "Dear Sir, we have seen in the newspaper that the rickshaw pullers' representatives He Wushan, Xu Zhulin, Feng Guisheng, Zhu Fengxiang, Wang Bowen, Cang Gongwen, Shan Tianfu, etc., have repeatedly petitioned your committee, which is very surprising. These so-called representatives are small vegetable stall vendors who were recruited by Zheng Fazhu to deceive your committee and have a great impact on the livelihood of rickshaw pullers. The publication of the new regulations was originally intended to relieve rickshaw pullers, but the rickshaw puller registration item stipulated therein has already been opposed by representatives Guoliang and others to your committee. At this time of rural bankruptcy and difficulty in making a living, once registered, it will increase the unemployment of more than 60,000 people, which does not seem to be the action that should be taken to relieve rickshaw pullers. Now, the so-called representatives are actually demanding registration, which is contrary to the original intention of the rickshaw pullers. It can be known that they are not rickshaw pullers' representatives. For the sake of the relief of rickshaw pullers in the city, we do not recognize the petition of the so-called representatives. We should state the detailed situation, so as not to be deceived by unemployed people. Please consider and handle accordingly."

Rickshaw Pullers' Representatives Publish the Truth

In order to clarify the truth, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency inquired with Chen Guoliang, the rickshaw puller representative designated by the Municipal Council, about the truth of the rickshaw pullers' representatives petitioning the Municipal Council Rickshaw Management Committee the day before yesterday (the 9th). Mr. Chen repeatedly denied that the rickshaw pullers had taken such a petition and said that the petition was entirely the result of a certain party's actions. The following is a record of his explanations: (1) Today (yesterday), I read in the newspaper that Xu Zhulin, Cang Gongwen, and others led more than 200 rickshaw pullers to petition the Rickshaw Management Committee. These representatives are not rickshaw pullers at all, so how can they obtain the qualifications of rickshaw puller representatives? Regarding the new regulations of the Municipal Council, they should indeed be approved, but the registration of rickshaw pullers is opposed by rickshaw pullers. There are a total of 10,000 rickshaws and more than 100,000 rickshaw pullers in the Special District. If the new regulations are implemented (four people per rickshaw), 60,000 to 70,000 people will be eliminated. In the current situation of rural bankruptcy and difficulty in making a living, once 60,000 to 70,000 people are laid off, the impact will be indescribable. Now, the so-called representatives are violating the will of the rickshaw pullers and demanding registration. Can this point be sympathized with by more than 100,000 rickshaw pullers? Otherwise, it must be determined who they represent. It is doubtful. I think our rickshaw pullers will never push out self-destructive representatives, which is a clear counter-evidence. (2) The so-called representatives have petitioned the Municipal Council a total of two times. The representatives are none other than He Wushan (also known as Heshan, Lingsheng, Lisheng, Songqing, Jiarui, and Hulin), Zhu Fengxiang, Wang Bowen, Cang Gongwen, Xu Zhulin, Shu Huajing, Feng Guisheng, etc. I have inquired with each small leader, and there are no names of these representatives among the rickshaw pullers. This point has already been reported orally to the Municipal Council Political Department this morning (yesterday morning). (3) After hearing this news, I immediately convened a temporary emergency meeting: (1) All points of the so-called representatives' petitions were denied. (2) Rickshaw puller registration was unanimously opposed. (3) Each rickshaw puller was notified to work in peace and not be used by anyone, etc.

Municipal Council Convened a Discussion Meeting

The Public Concession Municipal Council attaches great importance to this matter. At 2:00 PM yesterday, it convened a discussion meeting with all parties. Superintendent McTing, Director Zhong Si, Political Department Robert Sheng, Rickshaw Committee Maxwell, and rickshaw pullers and owners attended. Zhong Si chaired the meeting. As a result, it was decided to strictly punish the saboteurs to maintain local security. All parties adopted cooperation and dealt with the situation unanimously. As for the arrest of Zheng Fazhu, Zheng visited Zhu Maocheng at 11:00 AM and was arrested by the Political Department. The current industry association has filed a lawsuit for crimes such as obstructing freedom. The police station is investigating the instigator. The petitioning rickshaw pullers held a meeting at 5:00 PM last night and resolved to send 40 representatives to advise people on each road to stop the sabotage today, etc.

Cheng Xiechun Firmly Resigns as Director

According to Cheng Xiechun's statement to a reporter from the New Voice News Agency, I attended the Municipal Council on the 6th of this month for the public rickshaw matter. Because the issue of changing regulations and obtaining licenses has been delayed for a long time, I am afraid that it has a great impact on the lives of workers and social security. Therefore, I did not hesitate to spend four hours participating in the final deliberation. I am deeply grateful for the understanding of all parties and the resolution of each issue. As for the candidates for the Rickshaw Mutual Aid Council, the gentlemen present unanimously elected me to take a seat, but did not state that I was a representative of the rickshaw pullers. Because I am old and troubled, I immediately resigned. Yesterday's newspaper reported that I was a rickshaw puller representative of the Mutual Aid Council, which is a joke. I sent a letter on the 10th at 4:00 PM to firmly resign.

McTing's Persuasion Results in Continued Business Operations

According to the New Voice News Agency, the rickshaw owners in the Special District decided to suspend business operations starting yesterday to cope with the unbearable harassment. Superintendent McTing of the Municipal Council was aware of the matter. Because it concerned traffic within the concession, he was sincerely afraid that it would lead to a major incident. He specially persuaded the industry association to continue business operations as usual and promised to provide strict protection. The rickshaw owners took the overall situation into consideration, so they notified each rickshaw owner at midnight to rent out rickshaws as usual.

Rickshaw Pullers Detour and Fewer Streetcars

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency specially went to various places yesterday to inspect. Detectives were densely deployed in various places, and there were no traces of these people. However, those in remote locations continued to carry out sabotage. When asked, the rickshaw pullers who were pulling rickshaws expressed resentment. Streetcars at the Xinshan Bridge, Shanban Factory, Xinqiao, Wuzhen Road Bridge, and other places have disappeared, and most of them detour. According to rickshaw owners, although they are still renting out rickshaws today, because of what happened yesterday, rickshaw pullers have stopped pulling rickshaws. In total, 5,000 rickshaws have not been rented out, so streetcars have become scarce.

Concessionaires and Others Petitioned Yesterday Morning

At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the concessionaires and small leaders in the Special District petitioned the Municipal Council, requesting strict arrest to maintain business operations. It was said that they were greatly concerned because yesterday's deflation caused problems with collecting rickshaw rental fees, which was of great importance and significance. They specially joined forces with genuine rickshaw pullers. The Municipal Council replied that they would strictly handle the matter. According to other sources, the Municipal Council did not pay attention to the rickshaw pullers' petition the day before yesterday, which supported Maxwell and other articles, because it was reasonable. After the arrest, they were released. Seeing that the harassment was increasing, they began to arrest severely.

Petitioning Rickshaw Pullers Held a Meeting Last Night

The Municipal Council Rickshaw Committee has started registering rickshaw owners since the 7th. Each rickshaw owner has gone to register. A reporter learned from the Rickshaw Committee yesterday that most of the rickshaw owners have completed registration since the 7th. The Rickshaw Committee will rush to complete the registration before the 15th according to regulations. It will also be open all day on Saturday. Also, Zheng Fazhu, who took the initiative to petition the day before yesterday, has been taken care of by the Municipal Council. The petitioning rickshaw pullers have scheduled a meeting at 7:00 PM tonight at the square at the intersection of Robert Sheng Road and Xiaoshadu Road to discuss how to respond.

Eurasia Company

Newly Purchased Giant Aircraft

Can Be Shipped to Shanghai by the End of the Month

According to the New Xin News Agency, in order to improve the comfort of passengers on the Ping-Guangzhou route and shorten the journey, Eurasia Airlines purchased a Junkers JU-52 all-metal giant aircraft from Germany in mid-April of this year for application. Yesterday, Mr. Li Jingcong, General Manager of the company, told a reporter from the New Xin News Agency that the new aircraft will arrive by the end of this month, and the advantages of the aircraft are quite detailed. The details are as follows:

Arrived by the End of the Month

Mr. Li first said that the Junkers JU-52 giant aircraft ordered by our company from Germany has a twin-engine three-seater, can carry 3,500 kilograms, can carry 30 passengers, and can reach Guangzhou from Beijing in just eight hours. It is the first time that China has used this type of aircraft. Recently, we received a telegram from the German side that the new aircraft has already been shipped to China and will arrive in port by the end of this month. At that time, it will be transported to Hongqiao Airport for assembly and then transferred to the Ping-Guangzhou direct route for application, so as to shorten flight time and benefit passengers.

Advantages of the Wing

The advantages of the wing of the giant aircraft are that the Junkers auxiliary wing is installed behind the wing, and its length is equal to the wing. When the wind is calm, even if it is fully loaded with 3,500 kilograms, it only needs to travel 270 meters on the ground to rise. After rising, the speed of flight in the air can be increased to 260 kilometers to 300 kilometers per hour by using this auxiliary wing. When landing, the flight speed of the aircraft can also be reduced to only 65 kilometers per hour. Therefore, even the JU-52 aircraft with a full load of 3,500 kilograms only needs to continue traveling 180 meters on the ground after the wheels touch the ground to completely stop.

Bankers Express

Savings Guarantees Are Difficult

According to the New Voice News Agency, since the promulgation of the Savings Bank Law, the banking industry in this city has generally believed that the articles in the law have many obstacles that are difficult to implement. After repeated meetings, it was resolved to submit a request for modification. However, the Ministry of Finance has already instructed each bank, according to the regulations in the first half of Article 9 of the law, to calculate the government bonds and treasury bills equivalent to one-quarter of the total balance of savings deposits at market prices and submit them to the Central Bank immediately as a guarantee for depositors. The Bankers Association also submitted a request for gradual implementation, which was rejected by the Ministry of Finance. The following is the opinion expressed by the banking industry to the New Voice News Agency:

Original Article 9. Article 9 of the Savings Bank Law stipulates that "Savings banks should deposit at least one-quarter of the total amount of savings deposits in the form of government bonds and treasury bills and other assets with guaranteed certainty in a special vault established by the Central Bank as a guarantee for the repayment of savings deposits." However, the previous ministry order only ordered each bank to deposit one-quarter of the equivalent of government bonds and treasury bills, without mentioning "other assets with guaranteed certainty." The banking industry believes that the implementation of laws and regulations should be entirely effective. Therefore, this time, the ministry approved that the types and numbers of assets with guaranteed certainty should be approved by the ministry at any time, and each bank should handle them accordingly. Currently, since the Ministry of Finance has not yet approved the types and numbers of reliable assets that can be guaranteed, it is difficult to first order the payment of one-quarter of the bonds. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency expressed the opinion that the regulations in this article do have difficulties, and the association should continue to request a delay in implementation, so as not to affect the public bond market.

Calculated at Market Price. The original order of the Ministry of Finance stipulated that the prices of public bonds and treasury bills must be calculated at the actual market price. However, public bonds and treasury bills are issued by the state and guaranteed by state tax revenue. Therefore, the recognized price should be calculated according to the face value minus the principal and interest that have been repaid, and should not be calculated at the market price. Because if it is calculated at the market price, it is equivalent to the government underestimating the value of national bonds, which seems unacceptable in law.

Guangdong Levies Import Tax on Domestic Goods

No Less Than a Disguised Restoration of Likin

The New Voice Society states that Guangzhou industrialists and merchants, citing the Shanghai factories and the fact that most are funded by foreigners, are using this as a pretext to dump goods in Guangdong. They are demanding that the Guangdong authorities tax all goods entering Guangdong from other provinces, regardless of origin. The Guangdong authorities have approved the request and have set up a bureau to collect taxes. Factories throughout the country are reportedly very resentful of this. Yesterday, this reporter visited Mr. Hu Xiyuan, a standing director of the China National Industries Federation, to ask for his opinion. Mr. Hu said that the Guangdong authorities' proposal to levy import taxes on domestic goods from other provinces will not only cause stagnation in the sales of goods from other provinces in Guangdong in the future, but also lead to a lack of coordination between production and sales in Guangdong itself, inevitably leading to rising prices and a higher cost of living. Moreover, this method of excluding goods from other provinces will, invisibly, create a spiritual division among the provinces, which will be extremely harmful to the future of the nation. Furthermore, various provinces have their own natural characteristics for both manufactured and local products. No single province can be all-encompassing and not need to seek goods from other provinces. For example, northern China's felt and Guangdong's gauzes have their own natural properties and specialized techniques that other provinces cannot compete with. If Guangdong levies import taxes on goods from other provinces, and other provinces follow suit, it would be no less than a disguised restoration of the corrupt likin system that has been in place for over seventy years. The adverse effects would be unimaginable. Fortunately, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Citizens' Association for Promoting National Products, and the China National Industries Federation have successively telegraphed the Guangdong authorities, offering earnest advice and requesting immediate cancellation. The China National Industries Federation will also telegraph Guangdong Province. Hopefully, Guangdong Province will not lack wise individuals who can accommodate public opinion and improve the situation.

In Ancient Donglu

District Court

Prohibiting False Rumors and Deceit

Civil and Criminal Lawsuits Based on Evidence

Solicitation and Manipulation Only Lead to Deception

The Jiangsu Shanghai District Court issued a notice stating that the court's handling of matters prioritizes discipline. Since taking office, the President and Chief Prosecutor of the court have always supervised and inspected, and there has never been any leniency. The current presiding judges and prosecutors in office were selected and appointed by the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and their integrity is credible. However, unscrupulous people often spread rumors and deceive people outside the court, claiming to be familiar with so-and-so and able to intercede, or claiming that if a certain amount of money is paid, a favorable verdict can be guaranteed. People are embarrassed by old habits and want to escape punishment or protect their own shortcomings, and often spare no expense to seek help, hoping to be spared. However, after the case is closed, they realize that they have been deceived. They are unwilling to file a lawsuit according to the law, or they attack anonymously, or spread rumors among themselves, and often conceal things, so the court has no way to investigate. Therefore, this notice is issued to inform the public that the court accepts civil and criminal lawsuits and handles them based on evidence and according to the law. Litigants should no longer solicit or manipulate the system, and be deceived and suffer losses. It is hoped that enlightened people will properly advise relatives and friends who have lawsuits to avoid spending money and being fooled. If there are unscrupulous people who go to lobby or impersonate court staff, they are defrauding people of their money. Victims should immediately arrest them on the spot or report them by name. Once the facts are verified, they will be severely punished. All should strictly abide by this notice. Issued on August 10, the 23rd year of the Republic of China. President Shen Xiqing, Chief Prosecutor Lou Ying.

Xiefeng Woolen Goods Store

Arson for Insurance

Quilt Soaked in Kerosene

Xue Xianggen Denies Being the Store Owner

Xiefeng Woolen Goods Store, located at 156 Hubei Road, is opened by Xue Xianggen from Wuxi with capital of 4,000 yuan. He has an insurance policy of 10,000 yuan with Ning Shao Insurance Company. Four months ago, due to poor business, the rent had been in arrears for three months. Xue then came up with the idea of soaking quilts, mattresses, stools, chairs, and other items in kerosene and piling them in a corner to set them on fire at 12:20 a.m. the other day, hoping to get a large amount of compensation. Within a few minutes, the fire had become fierce. The neighbor Xin Gong Yang Woolen Goods Store discovered it and immediately reported it to the Central Fire Brigade by telephone. The fire was extinguished after the fire engine arrived and worked hard to put it out, fortunately without affecting the neighbors. Afterwards, the local Laozha Police Station, Hua Detective Pang Ruiqing, He Renrui, Western Detective, and others, together with the Western fire chief Haka Si Er, inspected the scene and found kerosene-soaked quilts, glass cups, and other items, and determined that it was arson for insurance purposes. They then found a way to arrest Xue. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Criminal Division 1 of the First Special Court. The police lawyer Gan Jingxian stated the case and prosecuted him under Article 187, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, and said that the police still needed to investigate, so he requested permission to postpone the hearing for one week. Then Haka Si Er and the Western Detective submitted a report on the circumstances of the discovery of the arson items. When questioned, Xue Xianggen stated that he did not open Xiefeng Store. The owner's name is Zhou Wenmei, and I am only a senior employee. This time, Zhou and a Yu, who makes a living from arson, discussed arson, and instructed me not to say anything and to replace the owner's name, promising me a generous reward, and said that if things were revealed, Zhou would turn himself in to the court and would not implicate me. Yesterday, Yu and two people with Shaoxing accents and one person with a local accent came to arrange things without letting me see, and told me to call for help five minutes after the fire started, but I was afraid of affecting the neighbors, so I told Xin Gong Store within two minutes and telegraphed the fire brigade. Judge Feng reviewed the confession and then ordered the case to be postponed for one week, and the defendant was returned to custody.

A Rubber-Soled Shoe Strike

Yu Shengfu Died Immediately

The Examination Confirmed Death Due to Heart Disease

The Police Requested a Judgment of Not Guilty for His Wife

Yu Shengfu, a Ningbo native residing at 390 Siwen Lane, Huade Road, was 46 years old. Recently, he was unemployed and lived at home, relying on his wife Xin to work at the Huasheng Cigarette Factory on the same road to maintain their expenses. Xin had been married to Yu for 15 years and had six children, three of whom survived: the eldest was eight years old, the second was five years old, and the youngest was two years old. Due to financial issues, the couple often quarreled, which was common. At 6 p.m. on the 26th of last month, Xin returned home from the factory and had another argument with her husband over trivial matters, which then turned into a physical fight. Xin took off her rubber-soled shoe and struck him once on the head, causing him to faint instantly and become unable to speak. He was sent to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment but died. The body was sent to the Pielu Road Mortuary for examination and embalming. Yu Xin was arrested by the Yulin Road Police Station and sent to the First Special District Court for questioning. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Yugui presided over a continued hearing in Criminal Division 3. The deceased had been diagnosed by a forensic doctor as having died from heart disease prior to death, which was unrelated to other matters. He then issued the examination report to the representative lawyer of the Engineering Bureau, Ru Bao Yi, for review and questioned Yu Xin, who was holding her two-year-old child and crying. She stated that her husband had fallen to the ground, and although she had slightly hit him with her shoe, it would not have caused his death. Her husband often slept during the day and suffered from heart disease without her knowing. She begged the court to see the truth. Lawyer Ru stated that the cause of death had been identified by experts as heart disease, and the defendant was not criminally responsible. Moreover, the couple had been married for 15 years and had three children, which shows their affection for each other. The three children are all young and depend on their mother for their livelihood. He requested that the court declare her not guilty. Judge Liu then appointed a lawyer to defend her pro bono and ordered her to be returned to custody for sentencing at a later date.

The Hairui Ship on the Way to Shanghai

Rescued Capsized Ship Crew

Seven Dead and Eight Alive

Survivors to be Transported to Shanghai Today

The recent Pacific typhoon affected both the northern and southern oceans. Various merchant ships took early precautions and suffered few accidents, but many civilian ships were sunk by the typhoon and waves. According to news from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday, the Hairui ship loaded passengers and cargo from Haizhou on the 8th of this month and set sail for Shanghai. After leaving the harbor, the ship was hit by a typhoon. The captain, seeing that the wind was too strong and the voyage was dangerous, returned to Laoyao. On the 9th, after the wind subsided, the ship sailed out again. At 9 a.m. yesterday, the Hairui ship was sailing in the sea area at 32 degrees 13 minutes north latitude and 122 degrees 23 minutes east longitude when it saw a large civilian cargo ship that had been hit by a typhoon and giant waves. They saw people floating on broken wood and saw the ship and asked for help. The captain of the Hairui immediately ordered the ship to stop and quickly lowered a sampan into the sea to help rescue them, and searched the nearby sea area for two or three hours. A total of eight shipwrecked sailors were rescued one after another, provided with clothing and food. The shipwrecked sailors said that the sailing ship they were on was registered in Qingdao and had license number 45. There were a total of 15 sailors on board. They were carrying cargo and unfortunately encountered a typhoon on Tuesday, the 7th, at 4 or 5 p.m. The ship was destroyed by the wind and waves, and all 15 people fell into the sea. They thought they would be buried in the belly of the fish, but now we have been rescued. There are still seven people missing, probably drowned, and they will inevitably be buried in the belly of the fish. These eight people were in the sea from the 7th until they were rescued by the Hairui, drifting in the sea for more than 30 hours, buffeted by the wind and waves. The Hairui is scheduled to enter the port this morning. After the eight people arrive in Shanghai, a decision will be made on how to send them back. It is said that all 15 people on the civilian ship were rescued, with seven drowning and eight surviving, which is true to the saying "seven dead and eight alive."

Public Concession

Work Summary of the Public Works Department

The Commissioner of Public Works' report for July states that progress has been made this month on the temporary detention center, cell block A and B, and the foreign inmate cell block at the Ward Road Jail. The reinforced concrete structure of the Central Police Station is complete and the walls and water pipes are being installed. A contract has been signed and construction begun on the Chinese constables' quarters at the Chengdu Road Police Station. The West Girls' Public School on Haineng Road and the Chinese Girls' Middle School on Singapore Road are largely complete. Three hundred and twenty-three private buildings are under construction this month. Two hundred and forty-four building plans were submitted, one hundred and twenty-nine were approved. Seventy-eight houses have been valued for property tax purposes. Three thousand four hundred and nineteen houses have been inspected. For sanitation work, 2,005 tons of dust and garbage were swept from the roads, 2.275 tons of objects were removed from the ditches, 1,796,000 gallons of water were used to sprinkle the roads, 2,040,800 gallons of water were used to wash the roads, 1.231 tons of household garbage were transported by truck, and 2.938 tons were transported by handcart, all of which were used to fill the low-lying areas in the east and west districts. 16.125 tons of garbage were transported by contractors by boat.

A Large Amount of Cosmetics and Perfume are Consumed

On Women's Legs

Progressive Women's Circles Will Also Advocate Banning Bare Legs

The import of perfume and cosmetics in the first six months of this year reached more than 850,000 yuan, which is an astonishing amount. Within the Public Concession

July Industrial Accident Statistics

According to the report obtained by the Municipal Council, there were a total of 121 industrial accident incidents in July, with 10 fatalities. Seven of the deceased were in the construction industry, while the textile, metal, and electrical supply industries each had one fatality. Among all the accidents, the causes of 106 were fully understood. There were 27 accidents involving powered machinery, fortunately with no fatalities; six electrical accidents, with one fatality and five injuries from burns; no deaths; 17 falls, resulting in four deaths; 30 injuries from being struck by objects, resulting in four deaths; during construction, one death was caused by a broken plank, and one serious injury. (One of the planks) was found to be insecure, leading to its breaking. Another young worker fell and fractured his skull due to an improperly placed board, resulting in death. Another worker carrying a bucket of ash fell from a ladder and died. In addition, two female workers were crushed to death when a factory building collapsed.

Tianyi Insurance Company

The Process of Recruiting Clerks

A Conversation with General Manager Liang Chenlan

China Tianyi Insurance Company, established with investment from leaders in the local financial community and well-known overseas Chinese, has enjoyed an outstanding reputation since its establishment. To expand its business and cultivate insurance professionals, the company is recruiting a number of probationary clerks in addition to its existing staff. The qualifications are limited to graduates from universities at home and abroad. Since the announcement of this news, applications for the examination have been very enthusiastic. The examination was held at the company on August 5th. The reporter, considering this matter to be of great importance to the development of the insurance industry and the career prospects of university graduates, visited Mr. Liang Chenlan, General Manager of the company, a few days ago to inquire about everything. The questions and answers between the two parties are recorded as follows: (Question) Why does your company require a university degree for this recruitment of clerks? (Answer) Insurance is a specialized field. A solid foundation is essential before appropriate training can be applied. (Question) Where do most of the applicants come from? (Answer) According to the review by the company's Recruitment Committee, more than 50 people were approved to participate in the examination. Graduates from well-known universities in both the north and south of the country, such as Tsinghua, Jinling, Guanghua, Fudan, St. John's, Soochow, Jinan, China, Daxia, and more than 20 other schools, have come to take the examination. (Question) What are the results of the examination? (Answer) Because the backgrounds of the applicants are different, the results are also different. Generally, those with liberal arts backgrounds excel in Chinese and English but neglect mathematics. Those with science backgrounds excel in mathematics, but their Chinese and English seem lacking. Those with law and political science backgrounds perform better in insurance studies, but are somewhat lacking in English and arithmetic. It is difficult to find someone who is proficient in everything. However, for the sake of providing opportunities for outstanding young people, our company has decided to select the best from the better and choose the most outstanding for cultivation. All hired personnel have been notified by letter separately, instructing them to report by August 15th. Those who were not hired but have expertise in one subject have also been informed by letter to bring their school transcripts for a face-to-face discussion with the company to find other ways to help them find employment. (Question) What are the benefits for probationary clerks? (Answer) The company has high hopes for these personnel and will provide them with fundamental training to enable them to acquire knowledge and experience and to advance with the times, gradually forming the backbone of the company. The first six months after hiring are entirely for training, because they have just left school and have no experience and cannot be assigned to any position immediately. During this probationary period, in addition to providing three meals a day, the company will provide a monthly allowance of thirty yuan to cover each person's transportation and miscellaneous expenses. After the six-month probationary period, positions will be assigned according to individual performance, or they will be sent to branches in other locations. At that time, all salaries will be handled in accordance with the company's official staff salary schedule. Mr. Liang finally stated that because the scope of our company is relatively large, in addition to handling fire, auto, accident, military, theft, silkworm cocoon, silver, and other insurances, we have also allocated a capital of one million yuan to specifically handle various life insurance policies, which has been deeply appreciated by all sectors. Business is developing rapidly, so there is a great need for talent. Looking at the insurance talent in the country, it is as rare as morning stars, so in the future, we can only actively train ourselves to meet the needs.

Dr. Zeng Baohan Departs for Overseas Study on a Regular Basis

To Study Bone Diseases in Europe and America

Dr. Zeng Baohan, director of medical affairs at the Shanghai Orthopedic Hospital and great-granddaughter of Zeng Wenzhenggong of Hunan, is scheduled to depart for the United States on the President Hoover this month. She is the first female doctor to go to Europe and the United States to study bone and joint diseases and infantile paralysis. Dr. Zeng has been appointed as the deputy director of surgery at the Lausanne Foundation Children's Hospital. The hospital gives such an important position to newly admitted doctors, which can be said to be extremely honorable. The biggest purpose of Dr. Zeng's trip abroad is to conduct on-site inspections of orthopedic and disability hospitals in Europe and the United States, and to learn about the latest treatment methods for these diseases in the world, as well as how to teach disabled children to adapt to future career choices, etc. Dr. Zeng is a top student from Jinling Women's University and graduated from Hangzhou Guangji

Female Doctor Zeng Baohan

Medical University. She served as a physician at the Shanghai Ximen Women and Children's Hospital. When Mr. Niu Huisheng founded the Orthopedic Hospital, she was hired as an assistant. For six years, she has devoted herself to the review of medical records, the treatment of surgical techniques, and X-rays, etc. As a result, Dr. Zeng's experience has become more abundant, and her surgical skills have become more refined. In order to seek further achievements and serve the motherland in the future, Dr. Zeng has made this trip. It is known that American orthopedic experts have sent letters to Mr. Niu, expressing their welcome and willingness to give her their full support. In addition, Dr. Black, chairman of the International War Wounded Treatment Committee in Boston and editor of the British and American Orthopedic Medical Journal, recently telegraphed Mr. Niu, expressing his willingness to plan everything for Dr. Zeng in the United States and in Europe in the future.

Robbery and Murder of Watermelons

Four Robbers Arrested

Specialize in Robbing Watermelons as a Regular Occupation

Surprisingly, there is an Account Book

Watermelon vendor Qu Atao was transporting watermelons from Huangdu to Shanghai. When the boat arrived at the west end of the Xinqiao Bridge at the Sampan Factory, he was robbed by many hooligans who boarded the boat and demanded watermelons and dragged Qu into the river, causing him to drown. It was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, it is known that the Second Squad of the Second Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau received a report at more than 8 am yesterday that the watermelon robbers were hiding on the boat in front of the Xintong Freight Yard at the west end of the Xinqiao Bridge in Guangfu Road. The team immediately sent police officers and arrested Ji Daxi, Ji Erxi, Ji Sixi, and Ge Maochun. After taking them to the team, they learned that the watermelons they had robbed were hidden in Ge Maochun's home. An account book for robbed watermelons and a pencil were found on the criminals, recording a large number of watermelons. It was learned that the criminals specialized in robbing watermelons for money, so they were all sent to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau for disposal.

Municipal Public Bonds

The Supervisory Committee for Use of Funds Was Established Yesterday

Organizational Regulations Approved by Executive Yuan Order

Sports Field Project Contract Approved by Municipal Government

The 3.5 million yuan Shanghai Municipal Public Bonds of 1934, since their issuance, have been organized into a Supervisory Committee for Use of Funds in accordance with regulations. The first meeting was held yesterday to announce the establishment. The details are as follows:

First Meeting

The Supervisory Committee for Use of Funds held its first meeting at the Finance Bureau at 10 am yesterday. The following people attended: Director of the Bureau of Education Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Bureau of Public Works Shen Yi (represented by Xue Cixin), Chairman of the National Debt Fund Management Committee Li Ming (represented by Lin Kanghou), Xu Yongzuo of the Municipal Council, Director of the Finance Bureau Cai Zengji, and Shi Wenjun of New China Company. The meeting was chaired by Cai Zengji, Director of the Finance Bureau, who reported: (1) The organizational regulations of this committee have been submitted to the Municipal Government and approved by the Executive Yuan; (2) The public bond funds have been paid in full as agreed and deposited into a special bank account; (3) The sports field project contract has been approved by the Municipal Government, with a total bid price of more than 870,000 yuan. It was also decided that meetings would be held every Monday afternoon at 3:00 pm on the first week of each month until 11:00 pm.

Organizational Regulations

Organizational Regulations of the Supervisory Committee for Use of Funds, Article 1: This committee is organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the Shanghai Municipal Public Bonds (hereinafter referred to as the public bonds) Ordinance of 1934. Article 2: The number of members of this committee is set at seven, allocated as follows: A. Director of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, B. Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works, C. Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, D. One person from the National Debt Fund Management Committee, E. One person from the Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council, F. One representative from the Shanghai Bankers Association, G. One representative from the underwriters. The members of the preceding paragraph shall be separately appointed by the Municipal Government. Article 3: The Director of the Finance Bureau shall be the chairman of the committee. Article 4: This committee shall hold a meeting once a month. If necessary, special meetings may be convened. Article 5: This committee shall exercise its supervisory power in accordance with the uses prescribed in Article 1 of the public bond regulations: (1) Reviewing the accounts of the use of funds, (2) Approving the payment of funds for use, (3) Reporting and publishing detailed figures of income and expenditure. Article 6: This committee shall be established from the date of issuance of the public bonds and shall end on the date when the amount of the loan is fully spent, reviewed, and approved for write-off. Article 7: After the establishment of this committee, it shall immediately report to the Municipal Government and submit it to the Executive Yuan for record. Article 8: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation by the Shanghai Municipal Government to the Executive Yuan. If there are any unfulfilled matters, they shall be amended by the Shanghai Municipal Government at any time and reported to the Executive Yuan for record.

Notice from the Finance Bureau

Collection of Land Value Tax in the North and South Districts

Collection set to begin on September 1

Deadline for Completion within Two Months

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating that the second phase of the provisional land value tax for the 23rd year, which should be collected in the first to seventh districts of the South Shanghai District and the first and second districts of the Zhabei District, is hereby set to begin on September 1 of this year. From the date of collection, the deadline for completion is within two months, ending on October 31 of this year. Those whose land is in the South Shanghai District should bring their receipts from the previous period and pay to the South Shanghai Tax Collection Office of the Bureau in Maojia Lane, South City. Those in the Zhabei District should bring their receipts from the previous period and pay to the North Shanghai Tax Collection Office of the Bureau on Datong Road, Zhabei. If the payment is not made within the time limit, in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Regulations for the Collection of Land Value Tax and Article 23 of the Implementing Rules, the case shall be summoned and recovered, and annual interest shall be added to the amount owed, and the proceeds of the land shall be extracted separately according to the years of arrears, and the land shall be auctioned off to compensate for the debt, in order to comply with the regulations and collect taxes heavily. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government and delivering the notice, it is hereby issued for the people to abide by it and complete the payment within the time limit, without any delay, so as not to be punished. Those who have not received the notice should, within the time limit, open the map number of the land location, the plot number, and the current address or contact address to the Bureau for a statement, so that a duplicate can be sent, and pay with the receipt from the previous period at the same time.

Discussions Between the Two Postal Associations

Reasons for Postal Losses

According to news released by the two postal associations yesterday, the China Times News on the 9th of this month carried a statement by a person in charge of the Postal Administration, which roughly stated that the post office lost as much as 10 million yuan annually due to the occupation of the four northeastern provinces, and that the annual increase in the salaries of postal workers nationwide was not enough to cover 15 million yuan. Now, according to members of the local postal associations, this statement is completely inconsistent with the facts. The losses of the Northeast Post Office are not as great as someone knows, and the salaries of postal workers have been very balanced over the years. Although junior employees have been recruited and promoted year by year, senior employees are also retiring and being eliminated from time to time. The reason for the postal losses is another reason: First, after the separation of the Savings and Remittance Bureau, the expenses were huge and the handling was improper; second, the Ministry of Communications ordered the post office to subsidize airlines indefinitely. It is heard that the two associations have prepared to ask the National Postal Conference to find a way to resolve it.

The Red Swastika Society Raises Funds to Relieve the Drought in Southeast China

This year, the drought in the southeastern provinces is disastrous, especially in the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui. The General Association of the Red Swastika Society has established a relief preparation office in Beiping and has begun to prepare disaster relief measures. The Southeast Main Association's Shanghai General Office has repeatedly received reports of disasters from Changzhou, Jiangyin, Jiangdu, Jiangpu, Gaochun, and other counties in Jiangsu, as well as Shangyu and other counties in Zhejiang, and Ningguo, Quanjiao, Wangjiang, and Huoqiu counties in Anhui. Generally speaking, the drought has been prolonged, organisms have withered, rural areas have collapsed, food prices have soared, and epidemics are prevalent. Every family is crying like cows, and everyone is sighing to the roof. The tragedy of the drought in Shaanxi and Gansu is about to appear in the southeast. In addition to sending notices to the various associations, the office has sent people to investigate the disaster situation in person, and has also sent notices to the standing supervisors of the various associations, and is scheduled to convene an emergency meeting on the 16th of this month to discuss relief measures.

Sixth District, Third Precinct

The Director Was Accused of a Case of Non-Prosecution

The Application for Reconsideration by the High Court Has Been Rejected

On May 28 of this year, the family of Mei Liujiang, a resident of No. 93 Meilong Town, West Shanghai, was searched for drugs by Liu Yin, a service worker of the Third Precinct of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and demanded 210 yuan. Film

The Central Theater Showcases "Dreams of the Old Capital" Parts One and Two. The Central Grand Theater on Sixth Avenue is screening "Dreams of the Old Capital" and its sequel "Further Dreams of the Old Capital," two films from Lianhua Film Company, totaling twenty reels, from today. There will be three daytime showings and two evening showings. This film is one of the most successful works of the national film revival movement of that year. All senior actors of Lianhua participated in playing key roles, such as Ruan Lingyu, Jin Yan, Lin Chuchu, Han Langan, Liu Jiqun, Zhou Boxun, Zhang Zhizhi, Luo Huizhu, Fei Boqing, Yin Meili, and more than twenty others, all of whom are included. Mei Lanfang also makes a cameo appearance as Yu Ji. The battle scenes are performed by soldiers of the 19th Route Army, using real guns and ammunition, creating a realistic scene. The entire play is divided into two parts, each with its own plot, which together form a perfect pair. It depicts the old warlords' exhaustive military pursuits, which are infuriating. It writes about heroic careers and love affairs, all of which can be thought-provoking. It is a masterpiece among domestic films.

Happy Forest Film Company Three New Films. Happy Forest Film Company released "Broken Mirror Reunited" at the Jin Cheng Theater three months ago, and new works have not been seen for a long time. In the past few months, the company has been working hard, dividing into groups, and three films are about to be completed one after another. The first film, "The Virtuous Wife," is directed by young writer Min Sai, written by Cheng Ziqing, and starring Xu Suzhen. The second film, "Female Prisoner," is directed by Wang Tianbei and written by Cao Pu. The third film, which is not yet completed, is "Three Daughters-in-Law," directed by Wang Tianbei, which depicts three types of women with different personalities. It is reported that the above three films will be released around the Mid-Autumn Festival.

Ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life are welcome to try it. Be sure to pay attention to the Ant Oil Ointment produced in Sweden.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the surrounding areas of Shandong are cloudy, with showers or fog in several places, and the wind direction is uncertain. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the area around here are sunny and hot, with Shanghai mostly cloudy and the wind coming from the southeast to the southwest. There are gentle southeast and east winds in the East China Sea. The weather in the Sea of Japan is bad due to a hurricane passing through and moving northeast. The hurricane in the Pacific Ocean is slowly moving northwest-west. The center of the first hurricane reached within 120 miles of the intersection of 17 degrees north latitude and 131 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, moving northwest-west. The wind force is unknown. The center of the second hurricane reached within 60 miles of the intersection of 39 degrees north latitude and 131 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, moving northeast. The wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 98.6 degrees and the lowest was 78.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 91.8 degrees and the lowest was 78.1 degrees.
